Accidental Fire in Flat Building Storing Medicines at Central Hospital 26

(Nanjing) A flat building storing medicines at the Central Hospital suddenly caught fire at 2:00 PM on the 21st. The losses are yet to be estimated. (21st Special Telegram)

Fire in Huludao, Nine People Buried in the Flames 27

(Tianjin) The fire in Huludao on the evening of the 17th started from the residence of a Japanese man named Okada. Due to strong winds, it spread to the surrounding neighbors, reaching 32 households. There was no fire brigade organization in the area. Japanese and puppet troops joined forces to use manual methods to extinguish the fire, which was finally extinguished on the morning of the 18th. The total loss is estimated to be more than one million. A British overseas Chinese woman and her young son, as well as seven Chinese people, were buried in the flames. More than 20 people were burned after jumping from buildings and rescuing belongings. Order was not restored until the afternoon of the 18th. (21st Special Telegram)

Japanese Establish Inner Mongolia Sheep Farming Cooperative in Duolun 28

(Beiping) Recently, the Japanese established an Inner Mongolia Sheep Farming Cooperative in Duolun and more than 20 Inner Mongolia Sheep Farming Cooperative branches in various important towns in Xilin Gol League, appointing the Mongolian traitor from Eastern Mongolia, Baoerda, as the general manager. The branch managers have not yet been fully appointed. Starting in mid-month, the Japanese also spent 28,000 yuan to purchase 3,000 Merino sheep in various leagues and banners of Chahar and distribute them to the Zaru and Luote Banners of Eastern Mongolia in order to improve the sheep breeds. Currently, a large amount of Japanese goods have been transported from Jinzhou to Duolun via the canal and are planned to be imported to various parts of Western Mongolia separately. (21st Special Telegram)

Survey of Japanese and Korean People Along the Beining Railway 29

(Beiping) The Japanese in Shanhaiguan have completed the survey of pseudo-civilians along the Beining Railway. In addition to the Japanese military police, there are 101 Japanese and 100 Koreans in Qinhuangdao, 10 Japanese and 7 Koreans in Haiyang Town, 1 Japanese and 7 Koreans in Liujiang, 7 Japanese and 10 Koreans in Shimenzhai and Yiyuan Kou, 17 Japanese and 7 Koreans in Funing, 4 Japanese and 9 Koreans in Liushouying, and 20 Japanese and 10 Koreans in Beidaihe. The total number of Japanese along the Beining Railway is 169, and the total number of Koreans is 150, totaling 319. Most of them are engaged in commerce. (21st Special Telegram)

Portuguese Envoy Arrives in Tianjin on Official Business 31

(Tianjin) The Portuguese envoy, Narvo Lou, arrived in Tianjin from Peiping at around 11:00 AM on the 21st on official business and will return to Peiping in a day or two. (21st Central News Agency Telegram)

Wang Jizong's Bandit Gang Plans to Advance North to Zunhua 32

(Tianjin) Wang Jizong's bandit gang, which fled to the outside of the pass, has not gone far and plans to advance north to Zunhua, disturbing the Santuntouying area. Villagers have gathered into groups and each household has drawn one man to provide weapons and defend day and night since the 19th. The magistrates of Qian'an and Zunhua counties considered the town important and have discretionarily dispatched one team of local militia each to assist. When Wang Jizong's bandit gang withdrew from Pianshiyu, they raped almost all the women in the nearby villages. After the rape, the bandits cut off their breasts or used bayonets to cut open their lower bodies, causing countless women to die tragically. (21st Special Telegram)

(Tianjin) Wang Jizong's bandit gang, which set up a camp in Pianshiyu, Zunhua, joined forces with Sun Yongqin's bandit gang from outside the pass and has gathered more than 400 people. On the 19th, Zhou Yuying's troops went to suppress them with machine guns. After a fierce battle for half a day, the bandit gang was unable to withstand and fled outside the Great Wall. In this battle, more than 20 bandits were killed and five were captured alive. Currently, the local militia is deployed in Diaoshan, Gaojia Zhang, and Songpengying to prevent the bandits from fleeing back. Wang Jizong's bandit gang has harassed more than 20 villages in the northern territory of Zunhua. Many men and women have been kidnapped. Santuntouying suffered particularly severely. Eleven farmers were killed in Qingmianyu Mashigou, two militiamen died, and the village chief was also executed by the bandits' guns. (21st Special Telegram)

More Than 50 Villages in Yutian Jointly Telegraph Requesting Allocation of Funds for Agricultural Loans 33

(Tianjin) More than 50 villages, including Daizhuang in Yutian, have lost all their seeds and agricultural implements due to local militia bandit disasters and have jointly telegraphed the provincial government requesting allocation of funds for agricultural loans as soon as possible. The 50 villages have more than 30,000 households in total, and they cannot resume their businesses without loan assistance. (21st Special Telegram)

Infectious Diseases Found in Two Counties in Hebei Province 34

(Tianjin) Scarlet fever has been found in Anci and Xingji counties in Hebei. Many men, women, old, and young are infected, and the infection is very rapid. More than 70 people have died of the epidemic in Anci and more than 100 in Xingji. Furthermore, this infectious disease has also been found in Taitouying in Hebei, where more than 20 young children have died. Schools in various places have suspended classes to prevent it. (21st Special Telegram)

Current Commentary

Welcome to the American Economic Mission 41

— Ren

The American Economic Mission, which has been the subject of much discussion in society, will arrive today. The members of the delegation are mostly leaders from American industrial and commercial circles. Both the head of the delegation, Mr. Forbes, and the deputy head, Mr. Carroll, are familiar with the situation in the East. This trip is expected to last two months in China. In terms of time, it cannot be said to be short, but in terms of its mission, it cannot be said to be insignificant. This trip not only has historical value for the friendship between China and the United States, but also may reveal a bright and promising path for the future of trade between the two countries. We respectfully and sincerely welcome these visitors from the New World and offer our views on the matter.

After the Crusades, trade between Europe and Asia became frequent. Westerners were generally aware of the vastness of Asia. When Marco Polo served in the Yuan court and returned to write "The Travels of Marco Polo," Westerners became even more aware of the wealth of Asia. The so-called "Asia" at that time was mostly represented by China, which was regarded as "heaven on earth" and called the "Golden East." At that time, Westerners came to the East mostly out of curiosity and adventure, rather than being concerned with the economic and trade policies of a country. Later, transportation technology improved day by day, making it easier to travel between East and West. With the catalyst of the Opium War, China's maritime trade restrictions were greatly relaxed, and more and more people from various countries came to China. China and other countries then established formal economic relations, making China a part of the world's economic currents, with shared interests and mutual concerns. In this historical evolution, although our international relations with the United States developed later, the people of both countries have always treated each other with sincerity and without deceit. Therefore, the relationship between China and the United States has always been considered harmonious, and has not changed in the past decade. Taking the trade relationship between China and the United States as an example, last year China's exports to the United States amounted to more than 94.4 million yuan, and imports amounted to 272 million yuan, ranking first among all countries importing into China. In terms of economic cooperation between the two countries, there were reforms proposed by Mr. Jingqi regarding China's monetary system, reforms proposed by Mr. Smith regarding Chinese railways, and a plan proposed by Mr. Ganmier regarding China's adoption of the gold standard. These points can all show that China and the United States have indeed had quite close economic relations.

In the past, China and the United States already had a deep friendship, and we naturally hope that this friendship can be preserved forever in the future. Therefore, within our capabilities, we should sincerely help the United States, and the United States, within its capabilities, should also sincerely help us. In recent years, China has suffered frequent disasters and persistent famines. Coupled with the impact of the world panic, the people's purchasing power has been very different from the past. As a result, foreign trade has inevitably declined sharply. Now that the members of the Economic Mission have come from afar, we sincerely hope that they will conduct a detailed study of this, using inductive methods and a far-sighted perspective to investigate the causes and current situation of the decline in purchasing power, as well as methods of assistance. The future of Sino-American trade is the most fundamental issue in the future economic relationship between the two countries. Whether there can be a new development in Sino-American trade depends on whether there can be a new increase in purchasing power. To do otherwise and seek the development of Sino-American trade on today's purchasing power would be tantamount to draining the pond to catch all the fish. This would not only be detrimental to China, but also unwise for the United States. In other words, under the current situation, what China feels most urgent is to increase the purchasing power of the people through economic construction. At present, we are constantly making our utmost efforts to create a "New China." However, if our friendly ally, the United States, can add its assistance to this, then China's purchasing power should be easily restored, and the development of Sino-American trade will also be promising. This is one thing we hope the members of the Economic Mission will pay attention to in addition to our welcome.

However, the United States is certainly not indifferent to the increase in China's purchasing power. For example, the purpose of raising the price of silver is nothing more than to raise the purchasing power of the Far East. However, this silver policy has been in effect for nearly a year, and judging from the facts that have already materialized, the results are the opposite of what the United States hoped for. Since the price of silver has increased, China's silver reserves have been flowing out continuously. As of now, the amount is approximately 400 to 500 million yuan. The occurrence of this kind of phenomenon was probably not anticipated by the United States at the beginning. Currently, China's total silver reserves are estimated to be 1.5 billion yuan. The daily decrease in China's silver reserves has not been accompanied by a reverse proportional change in the purchasing power of the Chinese people. If the silver, the means of purchasing, is completely drained, there is bound to be a major upheaval in China's monetary system. This will not only be unhelpful to the development of Sino-American trade, but may even cast a shadow over the decades-long future of Sino-American friendship. This is the second thing we hope the members of the Economic Mission will pay attention to in addition to our welcome.

Today, the members of the Economic Mission are all people who have directly or indirectly interacted with China on a regular basis. Therefore, we firmly believe that their investigation and research will definitely achieve great success. In the future, when they return, they will not only influence the American business community, but China will also be affected. Helping others is helping oneself. We are very willing to help the United States, and the United States should also help us. Therefore, we sincerely hope that the mutual assistance and prosperity of the economies of China and the United States can have a further development after this Economic Mission's investigation.

Volcanic Eruption in Japan, Violent Earthquake in Taiwan, Epicenter North of Taichung, Thousands Dead and Injured, Countless Houses Destroyed 42

Komoro, 20th. At 4:22 PM, Mt. Asama suddenly erupted with a loud sound, and at the same time, lava erupted, with black smoke rising into the sky. It was even more intense at night. Even in the distant Takasaki area, the ashfall was very heavy. In the Karuizawa area, stones fell like rain, temporarily disrupting traffic. The scene was extremely bleak. The state-owned forest in Konuma Village was set on fire by falling lava, and the fire was very fierce. The sky was ablaze, and the fire burned for nine hours before it was extinguished at 11:00 PM. The damage to the foothills was very severe. The extent of this eruption can be compared to that of 1929. The smoke rose 12,000 meters above sea level, making it a rare and spectacular sight in decades. (United News, 21st)

Taipei. The entire island of Taiwan and the Penghu Islands experienced two strong earthquakes this morning at 6:02 AM and 6:27 AM. The magnitude of the earthquake was 60, making it the most severe earthquake in decades. The epicenter was located in the upper reaches of the Huangliu River in southern Hsinchu Prefecture. The damage in various places is very severe. Railways were destroyed, iron bridges were broken, and tunnels collapsed in a total of 25 locations. Telecommunications were disrupted. The most severely affected area was Hsinchu Prefecture. The damage in Taichung Prefecture was also great. A large fire broke out in Shimizu Street, and the ground nearby cracked, spewing out mud. The damage in Taipei and Tainan Prefectures and the eastern coast was relatively light. (China United Press, 21st)

Taipei. At 6:00 PM on the 21st, the Taiwan Governor-General's Police Bureau announced the following:

The most severely affected areas are Neipu Village in Fengyuan County and Shimizu Street in Dajia County. (Dentsu, 21st)

Taipei. The damage from the earthquake in the Taichung area this time is beyond expectations. Communication organs in the affected areas have lost contact with various parties, making it difficult to determine the details. However, the number of people crushed to death has reached more than 3,000, and the affected areas number 30. Due to the lack of communication organs, rumors are spreading everywhere. The Governor-General's Office has contacted the Taiwan Army Command to make efforts to suppress the wavering public sentiment. (Dentsu, 21st)

Report from the Meteorological Observatory

(Tokyo) The Central Meteorological Observatory issued the following report regarding the violent earthquake that occurred in Taipei this morning: At 8:02 AM (Tokyo time) on the 21st, the entire island of Taiwan felt an unusually severe earthquake. Taipei and Taichung were moderately affected, while Tainan and Mount Ali were only slightly affected. The shaking was most intense in Hsinchu and Taichung Prefectures, and there is likely to be considerable damage. It is noted that the last major earthquake in Taiwan occurred in Chiayi Prefecture in March of 1906, with 1,300 deaths. More recently, there were earthquakes in the Taichung area in December of 1930 and in the Yilan area in August of 1934, but the damage was not significant. (United News, 21st)

(Tokyo) The Central Meteorological Observatory further reported on the earthquake in Taiwan as follows: The epicenter of the earthquake in Taiwan this morning was likely in the area of the lower reaches of the Daan River in Hsinchu and Taichung Prefectures. The depth of the epicenter was very shallow, about ten kilometers below the surface. Because the epicenter was shallow, the shaking was limited to a local area but was extremely intense, resulting in significant damage. A considerable number of aftershocks are still expected in the future, but the situation is gradually calming down. (United News, 21st)

Taichung Suffers the Greatest Damage

Taipei. Among the damages caused by this morning's earthquake, Taichung Prefecture suffered the most severe damage. As of 1:00 PM today, the number of deaths in Fengyuan County reached 1,039, with 3,202 seriously injured. In the Shimizu Street area of Dajia County, more than 1,500 bodies have been found as of 1:00 PM, and the situation is tragic. 631 houses were completely destroyed and 76 houses were half-destroyed. It is feared that the damage in other areas is also very severe. Due to the disruption of communications, the details are unknown. The Taipei Governor-General's Office dispatched rescue teams immediately after receiving the report and is currently rushing sanitary materials and other items. (Dentsu, 21st)

Taipei. The epicenter of the earthquake this morning was in Taichung, which suffered severe damage. In addition to the collapse of the railway bridge between Fengyuan and Houli, many other sections of the railway were also damaged. In Dajia, a fire broke out, and the losses are incalculable. The telegram and telephone communications to Taichung are almost completely destroyed. Repairs began at 9:16 AM, and the only connection currently working is the one between Taipei, Taichung, and Hualien. The sixth and seventh tunnels on the mountain line of the Taiwan Longitudinal Railway have cracked, and the inside of the eighth tunnel has collapsed. (Dentsu, 21st)

Taipei. The damage to the railways from this earthquake is unprecedented. There were 25 locations where bridges were destroyed and tunnels cracked, collapsed, or caved in. Many iron bridges were dislodged, making it impossible to restore the mountain line for the time being. The coastal line tracks have collapsed in many places. Germany Protests League of Nations Resolution, Three Countries Remain Silent, Unexpectedly Mildly Worded German Dispatch, Leaving Room for Future Negotiations 46

(London) The German government's short dispatch opposing the resolution passed by the League of Nations Council condemning Germany's rearmament has not caused turmoil in the capitals of the three major European powers: Britain, France, and Italy. Major British cabinet members have gone out to enjoy the Easter holiday, so the German dispatch will not be considered until after the holiday is over. Politicians in France and Italy have not expressed surprise at Germany's actions. It is reported that Paris does not want to respond at present because Germany has indicated that it will have another protest. According to a French government spokesman, the German dispatch is not important and does not need to be criticized. Rome has published the German dispatch, but officials and newspapers have not commented on it. It is believed that the Italian government is also waiting for Germany to present its second protest before issuing an opinion. According to the German dispatch, it is protesting the League of Nations' resolution condemning Germany. This dispatch was sent to the 14 countries related to the League of Nations' resolution, but the dispatch to Denmark was mild in tone, stating that the German government specifically sent this dispatch to inform the Danish government that Germany had sent dispatches to other countries. When the League of Nations Council voted, the Danish representative abstained from voting in favor of condemning Germany. (Reuters, 21st)

(London) The German dispatch opposing the Geneva resolution is still the focus of the world stage today. Rumors are rampant in the capitals of various countries. However, most people believe that this response from Germany is more to appease the anger of the German people than to deal with other countries. Paris and Rome both believe that it is not worthy of attention. Although Japan calls it "an absolute rejection of the League of Nations' actions," it also says that "the door to future discussions has not been closed." Officials here feel that between the lines, the German diplomatic community still intends to return to the League of Nations. However, at the same time, Germany will also adhere to its original intention of maintaining its rearmament plan regardless of the Treaty of Versailles. French officials stated today that the Geneva resolution was a collective action of the Council, so countries can only file Germany's protest and cannot take any other actions. (National News, 21st)

(Berlin) According to diplomatic sources, Germany may still participate in the various international negotiations currently underway. The protest that Germany lodged with the United Kingdom, France, and Italy this afternoon due to the resolution of the League of Nations Council was generally expected to be very rude and inconsistent with diplomatic practice. However, it was not so after it was issued, which shows that leader Hitler accepted the advice of the diplomatic authorities and issued it in a moderate form. In that case, the possibility of Germany participating in international negotiations has been preserved by the diplomatic authorities. (Havas, 20th)

(Berlin) Newspapers are attacking the League of Nations, and although their tone is arrogant, their words imply that Germany has reserved room for future negotiations in its protest. For example, the Berliner Tageblatt said, "The people of Geneva are acting blindly, and we should guide them. Our German neighbors are seeing ghosts in the shadows, and we should inform them." (Havas, 21st)

(Paris) Newspapers commented on the German protest, saying that the wording was intense but not as extreme as expected. Le Petit Parisien said, "There are those on Hitler's left and right who advocate moderation, and those who advocate radical action. Looking at the protest, it is clear that the moderates have prevailed." Le Petit Journal did not attach much importance to the German protest, saying, "Its purpose is only to express its views and not to remain silent. As for Germany's true answer and true defense of the League of Nations' resolution, the competent authorities are drafting it." The Les Echos' tone was similar, and it said, "What is unknown is what Germany's so-called expression of its position is." Le Figaro said that the reasons cited by Germany have no value in law, and the so-called Council resolution is a kind of differential treatment, which is even more inexplicable. However, "in terms of the wording of the protest, it is clear that Germany has no intention of rejecting negotiations." (Havas, 21st)

(Berlin) Today is the 46th birthday of the German leader, Hitler. Quoting Bismarck, Russian Newspaper Warns Germany 49

(Moscow) Izvestia published an article entitled "Warning," detailing the discussion and resolution of the League of Nations Administrative Council, and pointed out that the Soviet Union has always opposed the Treaty of Versailles. It said, "All financial, economic, and military deceptions in the Treaty of Versailles have now been abolished, and the powers with historical responsibility for the treaty have also acknowledged this, and since the treaty can no longer be forcibly restored, it can be seen that the treaty has become a useless burden. However, the powers have further raised the question of 'what can be done in the future?' This question is extremely important politically, and the League of Nations Administrative Council has resolved to warn Germany, accusing it of unilaterally destroying the European status quo and causing people to step into a cruel war in the future. Germany is eager to change the few remaining territorial clauses of the Treaty of Versailles and wants to realize its open aggressive plan to expand its territory. All of this is a threat to the world, and the members of the League of Nations (including Denmark) have all acknowledged this. All the allied countries in their resolutions have unanimously stated that they are willing to take defensive measures against Germany's actions to disrupt peace. The resolution unanimously passed by the Administrative Council is a great political event. We must not ignore its significance. Although Fascist Germany has various means of threatening its neighbors, Bismarck had warned in the past not to underestimate the 'insignificant elements' in politics. At present, most countries believe that Germany is threatening peace, so they must find ways to defend themselves. This belief is what Bismarck called 'insignificant elements.' Once this element is tested, it can always turn into millions of tons of steel and hundreds of millions of people fighting to defend peace. At present, this public opinion is extremely powerful, so Poland and other countries have to join (at least join the voting) in warning Germany. The Soviet Union's support for the resolution of the League of Nations Administrative Council is not out of any hostility towards the German people, but based on its consistent peace policy. If the German government can understand the significance of this warning and understand that all its aggressive steps can only strengthen other countries to take more resolute defensive measures, then it will come to the conclusion that it must create a collective security system in fact, not just in words. This conclusion will be welcomed by the Soviet Union," (TASS dispatch on the 20th).

Russian Ambassador to the US Speech Discusses War Crisis: Once It Erupts, It Will Affect the Whole World, Russia Is Willing to Cooperate with All Countries to Maintain Peace 50

New York News: The Soviet Russian Ambassador to the United States, Mr. Troianovsky, recently gave a speech at a luncheon at the Pond Club in New York, stating that the growth of the war crisis has become increasingly obvious. Even those who do not want to see this crisis cannot pretend not to see it. Perhaps Americans are still hesitating and examining, but those of us who live in dangerous areas already deeply feel the urgency of the situation. I do not believe that anyone with access to information hopes to limit the scope of a new war to Western Europe, Eastern Europe, or Southern Europe. If a future European war occurs, it will definitely not be localized but will become a universal and large war, the largest of all major wars. And because of the continuous invention of new weapons, the barbarity and cruelty of this war will also be unprecedented. Not only soldiers on the battlefield but also civilians far from the battlefield will be attacked by poison gas and from the air. Entire cities and villages will be destroyed. The destruction of resources and the decline of civilization cannot be quantified. It can be declared without hesitation that my Soviet Union is being forced to consider the situation from our special perspective, that is, the force of events has forced us to prepare for the worst. We are prepared to protect the integrity of our country's territory and even the lives and property of our people. Mr. Troianovsky stressed that the Soviet Union does not want war but is willing to cooperate with other countries as much as possible to ensure and consolidate peace. He also said that if the traditional diplomatic methods are not suitable for today's use, then new methods must be sought to maintain peace. In his opinion, even if the governments of various countries cannot guarantee a peaceful outcome for the current crisis, they should at least promise not to provide assistance to countries that provoke aggression. Although this is just empty words, it can also give the "violent troublemakers" the power of sanction. (World Press)

Great Contribution to Medicine: Internal Organs of the Human Body Can Be Filmed 59

(Paris) In the future, the various organs in the human body can be filmed and projected on the screen for research. This amazing invention is the result of hard work by French Doctor George. The method is to use several non-arc-shaped lenses, which are combined to form a lens with extraordinary luminosity and equal to the speed of ordinary films (i.e., 16 images per second). It can be used to film the internal organs of the human body. From now on, what doctors can see when examining patients is no longer the static state of the organs but the working state of the organs, which will inevitably be more accurate. For example, the flow of blood in the pulse, the enlargement of the trachea, the contraction of the diaphragm, the operation of the stomach, and the absorption and digestion of food can all be filmed and examined. Letter 73

Re: Letter from the Hebei Post Office Regarding the report in your newspaper's Special Dispatch column on March 27th of this year, which stated that the people's militia resisting orders in Yutian were defeated by the security team. It also stated, "The Yutian Post Office has compiled statistics showing that the security supplementary team stationed in the county extorted property from wealthy households and remitted it abroad, amounting to more than 1,267,000 yuan in the past year. Among them, remittances from Japanese and Korean drug foreign firms accounted for the most, totaling several hundred thousand." We have investigated in detail and found that the Yutian Post Office does not have such statistics. The total amount of remittance business for the entire year of the 23rd was only tens of thousands of yuan, which does not match the situation published in your newspaper. We believe that it is a misrepresentation of rumors and should be corrected to show the facts. We would be very grateful.

Hebei Postal Administration, to the Shanghai Shen Bao, April 19th

Gu Mengyu Arrives in Beiping, to Rest and Recuperate in a Different Place as Advised by His Doctor, Yin Tong Has Also Returned to Beiping 74

Beiping Correspondence: Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu and Director of the Beining Railway Bureau Yin Tong arrived in Ping one after another this morning (20th). Gu came north to recuperate. He took the Shuntian wheel from Shanghai along the sea route north a few days ago. He arrived at Tanggu at 5:00 this morning (20th) and transferred to a special train specially prepared by the Beining Railway Bureau to travel west. He passed Tianjin at 7:40 and arrived at Qinghua Garden Station at 11:00. He transferred to a car and went straight to Huanshan Valley in the Western Hills to rest. In addition to his wife and children and attendants, there were also Shen Chang, Director of the Ping-Sui Railway Bureau, and Zheng Zhao, Deputy Director of the Beining Railway, who accompanied Gu to Ping from Tanggu. Gu did not meet with any visiting guests except for Yin Tong, the Director of the Beining Railway Bureau, whom he met for a brief conversation. Shen Chang, the Director of the Ping-Sui Railway Bureau, told the press at the Railway Bureau at 3:00 this afternoon (20th) about the reason for Gu's trip north, "Minister Gu suffered from insomnia before. After being cured, he was advised by his doctor to rest and recuperate in a different place, so he made this trip north. He does not have any mission. He is scheduled to return to the capital at the beginning of next month to report for duty. On the way back to the capital, he may inspect the railway affairs of various lines." Yin Tong came to Ping to prepare for a sightseeing trip to Japan and to deploy the work of clearing up the "war zone." According to Yin, who told reporters at the East Station waiting room, (1) Chairman Huang (Fu)'s health has recovered and he has gained weight. He may come to the capital at the end of this month or the beginning of next month to take up the post of Minister of Interior. In the future, he plans to travel back and forth between Beiping and Nanjing to take care of the political affairs of both the north and the south. (2) After the replacement of the security team in the "war zone," the issue of command is clearly stipulated in the organizational regulations of the two district commissioners' offices, that is, the commissioners have the power to command the security team, so there is no problem with the commissioners commanding the security team. However, there is no preparation for the establishment of a security command. (3) The issue of the continued existence of the "war zone" clearing committee after the statutory time has expired was not discussed when I met Chairman Huang. Therefore, this matter will be discussed at a plenary meeting of the committee and then reported to the higher authorities for a decision. (4) I will not stay in Ping for long. I am scheduled to go to Tianjin on the 24th and lead specialized personnel from the Railway Bureau out of the pass from Tianjin, passing through Shenyang, Andong, Korea, and other places to Japan to participate in the sightseeing conference of the Japanese Ministry of Railways, which opens on May 2nd. The conference will last for ten days and is scheduled to close on the 12th. After the conference, we will investigate railway administration in Japan and then return to China. (5) I visited the central government officials in the capital and reported on the recent situation in the north. The central government is very clear about the situation in North China and expressed its appreciation for the clearing work in the "war zone." (6) I heard that Minister of Railways Gu came north to recuperate. Because I did not meet Gu in Shanghai, it is difficult for me to answer how long Gu will stay in Ping. (20th)

Security Bureau of Hubei Province Uncovers a Major Embezzlement Case; Section Chief, Division Chief, and Accountant Implicated; Mastermind Yu Taoshen Sentenced to Death 75

Hankou Dispatch: The Security Bureau of Hubei Province discovered a major embezzlement case last year. Section Chief Yu Taoshen was the mastermind, with Division Chief Wang Xuejun and Accountant Zuo Hexuan as accomplices. At the time, Fan Xiji was the director. After the incident came to light, Fan secretly reported to Zhang Qun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, who then forwarded it to the former Pacification Headquarters of the Three Provinces (Hubei, Henan, Anhui). The headquarters dispatched personnel to jointly investigate the case, while Fan resolutely resigned to show his responsibility. The case has now been investigated and clarified, and the official verdict was announced on the 19th. The details of the case's origin and the judgment are recorded as follows: Initially, Yu Taoshen, a colonel and section chief of the Fourth Section of the bureau, colluded with Division Chief Wang Xuejun and Accountant Zuo Hexuan to embezzle funds. The scheme remained undiscovered for a long time, but rumors spread widely, eventually reaching Director Fan Xiji. However, lacking solid evidence, Fan could only investigate secretly. On the morning of August 11th last year, Yuan Guilin, a service soldier of the bureau, stole 21 packages of military supplies from the repair shop warehouse, including 390 old military blankets, 390 leg wraps, 144 new military hats, and 559 new gray military uniforms. In the afternoon of the same day, he stole another 20 packages of military supplies from the Security Bureau warehouse, including 1,887 new and old bedsheets and 100 sets of new cotton military uniforms with military hats. He transported these items to the Xinyilong Military Uniform Store and deposited them with Zhu Kaixuan. Upon receiving the report, Fan Xiji dispatched soldiers to the store the next morning, recovering all the stolen military supplies and arresting Yuan Guilin. Yuan confessed that he was acting under the orders of Section Chief Yu Taoshen, Division Chief Wang Xuejun, and Accountant Zuo Hexuan. Yu and Zuo immediately fled upon hearing the news, leaving only Wang Xuejun to be arrested. The bureau reported the matter to the provincial government. Zhang Qun, Chairman of the Provincial Government, reported it to the Pacification Headquarters of the Three Provinces. The headquarters, together with the provincial government and the bureau, jointly dispatched personnel to investigate the case. All related parties were summoned for questioning. It was also discovered that in addition to stealing military uniforms, Wang and others had also engaged in the malpractice of withholding equipment and embezzling public funds. The most conclusive evidence was found in two matters: First, in May of the 22nd year of the Republic, an application was submitted to receive five items—canteens, dry food bags, bullet belts, rifle slings, and backpack frames—for the headquarters and various regiments. Yu Taoshen and Zuo Hexuan prepared a preliminary budget, issued false receipts for goods received, and exchanged them for fake receipts from the Xinkang Company military uniform store to claim funds from the treasury, receiving 8,407 yuan and 20 cents. Second, in the case of summer uniforms issued to the headquarters in the 23rd year of the Republic, a preliminary budget was prepared, and receipts from the Xinyilong Military Uniform Store were obtained by Yu Taoshen and Wang Xuejun. Among them, for the item of coarse cloth shoes, the preliminary budget was for 13,346 pairs, but only 3,026 pairs were actually purchased. For the remaining 10,320 pairs, Yu Taoshen and Wang Xuejun issued false receipts for goods received, exchanged them for fake receipts from the Xinyilong Military Uniform Store, and claimed funds from the treasury, receiving 6,708 yuan. For both of these matters, there were no receipts from the headquarters or various regiments, indicating that the items were never manufactured or issued. Yu Taoshen embezzled the funds alone. Other criminal circumstances that were not proven were not considered. Based on these two cases alone, Yu had embezzled over 15,000 yuan, a very serious offense. After collecting evidence and thoroughly investigating the confessions, the judges determined that Yu Taoshen, Wang Xuejun, and Zuo Hexuan had jointly stolen military uniforms, withheld equipment, and embezzled public funds. The evidence was conclusive and undeniable. Yu Taoshen was the mastermind, guilty of both crimes. Therefore, in accordance with the Regulations on Rewards and Punishments for Civil and Military Officials and Soldiers in the Bandit Suppression Area, the Military Criminal Law of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, the Military Trial Law of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, and the Criminal Law, he was sentenced to death. Upon capture, he will be executed by shooting, and all his property will be confiscated to compensate for the losses. Zuo Hexuan and Wang Xuejun were subordinates of Yu, following his orders, and Yu had absconded with the public funds. Their criminal circumstances were deemed deserving of leniency, and their death sentences were reduced by half. Zuo Hexuan was sentenced to 14 years of imprisonment, and Wang Xuejun was sentenced to 12 years of imprisonment, both with deprivation of civil rights for 20 years. The case is now closed. (20th)

Construction Bureau of Anhui Province Organizes Scenic Spots in Caishi; Cui Luo Mountain Developed into a Park; Plum, Bamboo, and Chrysanthemum Planted All Over the Mountain 76

Wuhu Dispatch: Caishi is located in Dangtu County, Anhui Province, close to the capital area and controlling the vital passage of the Yangtze River. Since the construction of the Jing-Wu Highway and the Jing-Wu Railway, transportation has become more convenient. Cui Luo Mountain stands tall by the river, with vast and boundless waters. The morning glow and evening sunset create a magnificent scene. Wild grass grows luxuriantly, and ancient pine trees are lush and verdant, offering excellent scenery and numerous historical sites. The burning of rhinoceros horns by Wen Qiao of the Jin Dynasty and the attempt to capture the moon by Li Bai of the Tang Dynasty are famous stories passed down through generations. The Construction Bureau, recognizing the increasing number of Chinese and foreign tourists visiting by car after the opening of the Jing-Wu Road, has specially ordered the Dangtu County government to enclose Cui Luo Mountain and develop it into Caishi Park to enhance the scenery and preserve historical sites. To save expenses and achieve quick results, a simple design is initially proposed as follows: (1) Transportation A. Roads: The section of Cai Xiang Road from the Caishi Station on the Jing-Wu Road to the entrance of Cai Xiang will be reinforced and leveled, approximately 100 zhang in length, leading directly to Caishi city. The streets within the city, up to the riverside and west to the foot of the mountain, will be demolished and widened to 2 zhang, and the surface will be converted into gravel. B. River Bridge: A wooden bridge with three openings, approximately 10 zhang wide and 4 zhang long by 2 zhang wide, will be built over the river, with earth filling at both ends to ensure unobstructed land and water transportation. C. Ornamental Archways: Concrete archways will be elaborately constructed at the entrance of the bus station and the park's main entrance to enhance the appearance. A wooden archway will be built at the park's rear entrance. D. Street Trees: Street trees will be planted along both sides of the road, using three-year-old new locust trees with protective frames to ensure they grow straight and easily survive. (2) Park Site A. Slopes and Stone Steps: Stone steps will be laid along the route from the park's main entrance to the San Tai Pavilion, through the ancient pine forest, and out of the park's rear entrance. Stone benches and tables will be provided at suitable locations for visitors to rest. Lamp posts will be placed throughout the area for nighttime strolling. B. Sports Ground: A sports ground will be built in the open space to the right of the park's main entrance, equipped with sports equipment. C. Planting Trees: Locust trees will be planted on the northwest side of the mountain, bamboo on the southeast side, tea trees by the river, plum trees on the south side of the mountain, flat grass around the Taibai Tower and the Three Dukes Shrine, chrysanthemums at the lower part of the south side of the mountain, and flowerbeds with various flowers and plants at the southern foot of the mountain. (3) Historical Sites A. Restoration: The San Shan Pavilion, located on the mountain peak with a panoramic view, is now completely gone, with only ancient steles remaining. It is proposed to build a palace-style stele pavilion on the site, retaining the original name. The Moon-Catching Terrace: Caishi is famous for the exiled immortal's attempt to catch the moon. The original site of the terrace is no longer extant. It is decided to build a semi-circular terrace on the original site, with steps leading up from the outside, providing a view of the river. Two rooms will be built below the terrace to provide shelter from wind and rain. B. Preservation: The Tang Taibai Tower has recently been renovated. However, the archway, bed, and other equipment are too few and will be added. Wen Qiao's burning of rhinoceros horns is also well preserved and will be slightly renovated. The ancient Emei Pavilion (i.e., Guanlan Pavilion) was recently built, but the ground is uneven and will be paved with concrete. The Guanyin Pavilion will be slightly renovated. The Sanyuan Cave and Yuxing Hall are still intact. The rugged roads will be repaired to facilitate visitors. (20th)

Jiangzhuang Town Robbery and Strike 78

Jiangzhuang Town in Punan is a sparsely populated commercial area. A public security team was originally stationed there, but it was recently transferred to Shanyang. Consequently, at about 1:00 AM on the 18th, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived in the town, carrying iron shovels, flashlights, and other items. In addition to reporting the case to the Public Security Bureau for investigation, all the shops in the town agreed to go on strike. It is unclear how this will be resolved.

Jiading: Illegally Established Licensing Tax Collection Office 79

Pu Tianqing, from Loutang in this county, used to be a businessman in Shanghai. A few days ago, he returned to Jiading to establish a county tobacco and alcohol licensing tax collection office. He rented Xiao Hanjiang's house in Gu Dian Lane in the city with a guarantee from the Tongmao Gong Flower Shop outside the West Gate. He also borrowed most of the internal equipment from Xiao. He hung up the sign of the tax collection office and prepared to collect taxes. The staff included five or six people, including Wang from Luodian. However, the collection of tobacco and alcohol licensing tax in this county had been handled by the Business Tax Bureau of this county since March 6th, according to an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance. Upon hearing this, Bureau Chief Wu Gengyang reported it to the County Public Security Bureau, which ordered the police to arrest Pu and escort him to the county government. During the interrogation, Pu confessed that he was entrusted by Qian Wanzong, a Shanghai resident, to handle the matter. Qian is the director of the county tobacco and alcohol licensing tax collection office and holds an appointment letter issued by Wang Ziliang, the director of the tobacco and alcohol licensing tax bureau of the five counties of Shangbao, Chuanjia, and Tai. He contracted the county tobacco and alcohol licensing tax for 8,500 yuan. Pu paid 150 yuan on behalf of Qian. The county government, considering that the statement seemed to have a basis, temporarily detained Pu and telegraphed the Department of Finance for instructions. On the 19th, a telegram was received from the Department of Finance ordering strict handling of the matter. It is clear that Qian and Pu illegally established the tax collection office. However, it is also heard that the appointment letter held by Qian is not entirely false, but it was issued in early February, when the Department of Finance had not yet ordered the Business Tax Bureau to concurrently collect tobacco and alcohol licensing tax. After Pu Tianqing was detained by the county, the staff in the office dispersed, and all the equipment, except for the borrowed items, was also moved elsewhere. After the county government received the reply from the Department of Finance, the Public Security Bureau again ordered the police to go there. Shen and two others were arrested together. Shen and others said that they saw the office's advertisement in the newspaper recruiting staff, applied, were hired, and paid a deposit. They had only come to Jiading to take office the day before.

Wuxi: Four Rural Temple Fairs Result in Bloody Tragedies 80

The day before yesterday was the 18th day of the third lunar month. The Furong Mountain festival in the fifth district of the county traditionally has a temple fair for morning pilgrimage. Villagers often engage in fighting to be the first to offer incense. The day before yesterday, incense associations from various villages went to the mountain to offer incense as usual. When the incense association from Xi Qi was about to enter the temple to offer incense in front of the Zhang Zhongcheng Temple, the incense association from Kenzhuang Bridge suddenly appeared. A conflict arose due to competition to be the first to offer incense. The thugs and swordsmen from both sides formally engaged in fighting, turning the mountain into a battlefield. The fierce battle lasted about half an hour before it stopped. However, the Xi Qi side suffered more injuries. Three people were seriously injured. One, Zhou Afu, was slashed four times on the top of his head and once on his shoulder, making him the most seriously injured, with his life in danger. Others, such as Zhou Fugen and Chen Baosheng, were also seriously injured. All three were covered in blood, a frightening sight. Also, on the day before yesterday, the combined incense association from Tang Lane and Zhang Lane near Liumenli in the ninth district came to Wuxi to offer incense at the Sanmao Temple on Huishan Mountain. Unexpectedly, the thugs from Zhang Lane planned to set up a boxing ring at the Zhonglie Temple with the swordsmen from Tang Lane to show off their skills, but Tang Lane refused, which angered the thugs from Zhang Lane. They immediately started fighting at the site. As a result, Tang Ronggen, a villager from Tang Lane, was beaten on the head, and blood flowed like a stream. Fortunately, the military police stepped forward to suppress the situation, and a tragedy was averted. Furthermore, a grand temple fair was held at Bashiqiao in Beixiang on the day before yesterday. The Public Security Bureau dispatched a mobile patrol team to the countryside to suppress the situation. Unexpectedly, when passing through Yandai Town, patrolman Song Tingbi was arguing due to the narrow road when suddenly a person punched Song's right ribs twice. Song felt dizzy and vomited blood twice. The team arrested the assailant, Zhu Genda, who has been taken to the bureau for interrogation. In addition, Madam Xi Fan, an old woman from Xinglong Bridge in the city, was watching the Sibao Bridge incense association at the West Gate the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, due to the crowd, she was pushed off the city wall, causing a hole in the top of her head more than four inches deep. She lost consciousness due to heavy bleeding. Although she was treated at the hospital, her life is still in critical condition.

Ordering Japanese Silkworm Eggs to Relieve the Silkworm Market 81

During this spring silkworm egg season, various fields in Jiangsu Province produced a total of more than 1.1 million sheets. Generally, silkworm egg merchants have been importing silkworm eggs into Zhejiang Province for sale, with a total of more than 500,000 sheets. Only more than 600,000 sheets remain in this province, resulting in supply falling short of demand. The silkworm mulberry model districts in various counties have established current sales offices at three locations, including the Wuxi Hotel, since the 6th of this month. Since the beginning of sales, the villagers who purchase silkworm eggs have been extremely crowded. As of 12:00 noon yesterday, all of the supply was completely sold out. However, those who arrived later were still extremely enthusiastic but felt disappointed. The deputy director of the model district, Zhou Yuanxun, considering the panic caused by the shortage of eggs, consulted with Tang Xixiang, the director of the Provincial Silkworm Silk Experiment Field, on relief measures. It was decided to purchase silkworm eggs from Japan to meet the emergency needs. After urgently telegraphing the province for approval, he quickly telegraphed Shanghai to contact the Japanese silkworm egg merchant, Jinzi. Jinzi immediately telegraphed his country to notify them to prepare for delivery and came to Wuxi last night to discuss everything with Deputy Director Zhou in person. It is reported that the price is one yuan per sheet, but the model district sells them to farmers for only forty cents per sheet. According to Deputy Director Zhou, the shortage of eggs in Jiangsu Province is not limited to Wuxi County. Counties along the Jing-Hu area also need to supplement their supply. Therefore, the quantity ordered from Japan has not yet been determined. Currently, it is temporarily assumed to be 100,000 sheets. The Japanese side has already replied to Shanghai. 3,000 sheets are expected to arrive tonight (the 22nd) to meet the market's needs.

Changshu: Lian Tang Temple Fair Causes Disaster 82

The Zhou Shen Temple in Lian Tangluo Township in the third district traditionally holds a temple fair in mid-March. The temple fair was held again on the 19th of this month, with all kinds of ceremonial guards. Therefore, the nearby villagers flocked there. Both vendors and ferry boats made ten times their usual profit. At about 2:00 PM, the villagers were very crowded. There is a ferry crossing there. Pedestrians must usually be ferried across. At that time, there were many male and female passengers on the ferry, including many young women. Some frivolous people were joking around in the boat. Due to uneven seating, the boat suddenly capsized. Fortunately, most of the men and women in the boat were familiar with swimming, and either swam ashore themselves or were rescued. Zhang Shigen's wife, Zhang, and a five-year-old girl drowned and died because they sank to the bottom of the river and could not be rescued in time.

Jiaxing: Large Gangs of Silkworm Raising in the Four Rural Areas 83

Silkworm farming in the four rural areas of Jiaxing has begun. The various silkworm industry guidance centers have already started to promote the germination of silkworm eggs. On the 19th and 20th, they distributed the silkworm eggs. A total of more than 96,000 sheets of silkworm eggs were distributed in the county. However, in the four rural areas, due to the private transportation of silkworm eggs out of the area, the silkworm eggs were sold to farmers at a reduced price, causing disputes. In the fifth district, most of the villagers were unable to purchase silkworm eggs for silkworm farming due to the severe drought last year. Therefore, fewer silkworm eggs were distributed. It is learned that after the villagers received the silkworm eggs, they started to harvest silkworm ants in large gangs on the 10th and 11th. Because the mulberry trees are very sparsely leafy, and the leaves are quite thin and the moisture content is normal, it is expected that the price of leaves will inevitably rise sharply in the future.

Stage Play Crushes Six People to Death 84

In Shengjia Township, where Jiaxing's northern rural area borders the Jiangsu Province, rural residents recently pooled their resources to organize a three-day spring opera performance starting on the 19th. The 21st was the last day of the opera performance. When the performance started in the afternoon, due to the crowd, some of the audience climbed onto the artificial rocks next to the stage to watch. As the artificial rocks had been piled up for a long time, the lower part was loose. At about 3:00 PM, when the gongs and drums were sounding, the artificial rocks suddenly collapsed, and the audience fled in panic. Several people were unable to escape and were crushed by the rocks. It is reported that six people were crushed to death, and many others were injured. After the incident, the opera performance was stopped immediately. The deceased were in a terrible state.

Jintan: Chen Kunshan Steals Electricity and Commits Assault 85

At 8:00 PM on the 15th of this month, Wang Xiaotong, an inspector of the Yili Electric Company in this county, and Wang Kouzi, a lamp installer, went out to check the lamps. While passing through Ximen Town, they found that Chen Kunshan's family had illegally installed electric lights. They immediately reported it to the First Substation of the Public Security Bureau nearby. The patrol chief, Yang Renlin, led a policeman to the scene together. Wang Kouzi was in the process of removing the illegally installed lights and handing them over to Chief Yang as evidence. Unexpectedly, Chen Kunshan suddenly led a group of security team members to the scene, forcibly took back the electric lights, and after beating Wang Xiaotong and Wang Kouzi, dragged them to the sub-team department outside the West Gate and hung them up and beat them for several hours before releasing them. At that time, Wang and others could not move. After the company was notified, they sent someone to take Wang and others to the public hospital for treatment. It is reported that Wang Jianzhong, the manager of the company, has filed a criminal lawsuit with the county government and plans to telegraph the Electrical Enterprise Federation and other groups to request assistance to achieve the purpose of punishing the perpetrators and obtaining compensation.

Zhenjiang: Jiangsu Anti-Smoking Association Establishes Factory 86

At the regular meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee on the afternoon of the 20th, only three members, Ye Xiufeng, Leng Yuqiu, and Xiang Zhizhuang, attended. A discussion meeting was temporarily convened, and many cases were discussed. Only a few decisions were tentatively made, and the rest were left for discussion at the next meeting. One decision was to establish a tobacco factory for smokers in the Nantong district. Leng Yuqiu reviewed the plan and submitted it to the meeting for discussion. The Provincial Anti-Smoking Association has now allocated 3,000 yuan as the factory's start-up expenses. The provincial association will also establish a canned food factory for smokers in the near future. The machines for manufacturing canned food can also be used to manufacture gas masks and other supplies. Its function can take care of both periods. Furthermore, to promote anti-smoking propaganda, the association plans to publish two publications: the Anti-Smoking Yearbook and the Anti-Smoking Newsletter. Both will be implemented at the beginning of the next year. The film script solicited by the association in the past has now received more than thirty pieces. Chairman Chen is very interested in this and has submitted it to the association for review. It will be transferred to the Central Propaganda Committee for selection. Because film scripts are different from ordinary scripts, the cinematography, scenery, economic factors, and time aspects must be considered. The Central Propaganda Committee has sufficient personnel for this and the selection is more meticulous.

Taixian: Lawsuit on Additional Taxes for Guiding the Huai River 87

In the Jiangsu Province's effort to guide the Huai River, the counties in the Huai River region collect labor, and the province subsidizes the workers' wages. However, many counties have added additional land taxes or collected per-mu donations to fund expenses related to guiding the Huai River. Huang Tong, from the Louzhuang Township Farmers' Association in Taixian County, previously filed a separate petition with the central government's relevant departments, requesting the revocation of the additional taxes imposed by the provincial government for guiding the Huai River and the illegal collection of per-mu donations by Zhang Yi, the magistrate of Taixian County, for the same purpose, and requesting that the county magistrate and others be handed over to the competent authorities for disciplinary action. This case has been repeatedly instructed by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, first ordering the relevant official departments to review the matter, and then ordering the Jiangsu Provincial Government to review and handle it. It is learned that Huang Tong continued to submit new evidence on March 20th of this year, presenting it to Premier Wang Chonghui of the Executive Yuan and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, concurrently chairman of the Guiding the Huai River Committee, for review. Both replies were received on the 12th of this month. (1) The Executive Yuan replied, "The submission is noted. As the matter concerns the Guiding the Huai River project, since it has been submitted separately, please wait patiently for the Guiding the Huai River Committee to review and handle it." (2) The Military Committee Chairman's Headquarters replied, "The submission and attachments are noted. Please order the Jiangsu Provincial Government to investigate and handle it."

Special Report

Investigation into the Circulation of Subsidiary Coins in Gansu (Continued) 88

— Zhu Jingzhou

(C) Exchange Rates of Common Copper Coins in Various Counties

The exchange rates of common copper coins vary across counties due to differing local conditions. For instance, in Jingtai County, one silver dollar can be exchanged for 5 strings of cash; in Jingyuan County, for 5 strings and 200 cash; in Gulang, Xiahe, Anxi, Minqin, and Pingliang counties, for 5 strings and 500 cash; in Wuwei County, for 5 strings and 800 cash; in Linxia, Yongdeng, Taosha, Yongjing, Lintan, Hezheng, Shandan, Yumen, Dunhuang, Yongchang, Gaolan, Dingxin, and Jiuquan counties, for 6 strings; in Ningding and Lintao counties, for 6 strings and 200 cash; in Zhangye, Minle, Haiyuan, Gaotai, and Jingning counties, for 6 strings and 500 cash; in Zhang County, Gangu, Huating, Huan County, Yuzhong, Huining, Tianshui, Wudu, Huixian, Min County, Liangdang, and Weiyuan counties, for 7 strings; in Wushan and Qingshui counties, for 7 strings and 300 cash; in Li County, for 7 strings and 400 cash; in Dingxi, Longde, Zhuanglang, Qingyang, Zhenyuan, Tongwei, Cheng County, and Longxi counties, for 7 strings and 500 cash; in Jingchuan County, for 7 strings and 750 cash; in Qin'an County, for 7 strings and 800 cash; in Huaping, Chongxin, and Kang County, for 8 strings; in Xihe County, for 8 strings and 200 cash; in Lingtai County, for 8 strings and 400 cash; and in Xigu, for 8 strings and 780 cash. Observing the varying exchange rates across counties, Jingtai County's 5 strings are the most expensive, while Xigu County's 8 strings and 780 cash are the cheapest. The difference between the two is 3 strings and 780 cash. The fact that such a phenomenon exists within the same province not only fully demonstrates the disorder of the monetary system and the obstruction of transportation but also provides an overview of the situation. What is even worse is that within the same county, copper coins may be commonly used in area A but not in area B, and vice versa. Min County is one example of this.

(D) Origin of Copper Coins in Various Counties

Regarding the origin of copper coins in various counties, except for 21 counties that did not report, the following is based on the 41 counties that did report. Among them, the most come from Sichuan, such as in Dingxi, Zhang County, Qingshui, Gangu, Lintao, Zhuanglang, Xihe, Wushan, Longxi, Huining, Wen County, Kang County, Wudu, Huixian, Qin'an, Min County, Xigu, Li County, Lingtai, Liangdang, and Cheng County. Those from the provincial capital and neighboring counties include Linxia, Wuwei, Xiahe, Lintan, Longde, Huaping, Jingtai, and Tongwei. Those from both Sichuan and the provincial capital include Jingchuan, Huating, Haiyuan, Huan County, Chongxin, Tianshui, Zhenyuan, and Li County. Jingning County receives its copper coins from the southeast, while Jingyuan and Pingliang counties receive theirs from Shaanxi. Yumen County receives its copper coins from Baotou and Suiyuan. In Sichuan Province, each defense zone freely mints coins, resulting in inferior coins worth 50, 100, or 200 cash flooding the market. Consequently, they have to rely on neighboring provinces as outlets. Longnan, which borders Sichuan, is the most severely affected.

(E) Copper Coin Notes and Cash Notes

Copper coin notes are circulated only in 10 counties: Taosha, Wuwei, Zhangye, Longde, Qingshui, Pingliang, Tianshui, Zhenyuan, Gaolan, and Cheng County. Except for Pingliang, which also uses copper coin notes from the Shaanxi Provincial Bank, the rest are issued by the Gansu Ping City Official Branch. The face value is mostly 10 coins, priced at 4 strings of cash per silver dollar. Since the provincial treasury has no intention of using this to supplement its funds, the amount issued is always determined by the market demand. With sufficient reserves and established credit, their exchange rate can even exceed that of the base currency they represent – copper coins. This is a unique phenomenon in Gansu Province and is unmatched by any other province. As for money shops and businesses issuing similar promissory notes, there have been no reports of such. The finances of various counties in Gansu are exhausted, and except for a few larger county towns, there is no organization of silver and money shops. Therefore, domestic remittances are extremely difficult, which is one of the reasons for the sluggishness of commerce. In the entire province, only Tian Shun Dang, Quan De Tang, Zhong Yi Hou, Wan Qing Cheng, and other shops in Jiuquan County issue oilcloth cash notes similar to promissory notes, totaling about 14,600 strings, circulating in the market. It is unknown when these originated, as there is no mention of it, making it impossible to speculate. Generally, the county is located in a remote western area, and funds are often insufficient. These cash notes were created in response to this need. However, their credit is still good, and the number issued is small. Once reorganized, there will be no problems. Although transactions in various counties in Gansu are still mostly based on cash as the unit, as a result of years of purchasing and recasting, cash coins have almost disappeared. Only in Minqin, Dingxin, Yongchang and other counties are some still used for small change. (3) Conclusion: In summary, the monetary evolution of Gansu Province is still stuck at the copper coin standard stage. There are two reasons for this: (1) Transportation in Gansu is inconvenient, the economy is backward, and monetary credit is not yet fully developed. In places like Dunhuang, there are still commercial systems of barter trading goods for goods. (2) People's lives are simple, and the amount of transactions is not large. The circulation of copper coins is most suitable for their economic background. Since copper coins are the center of transactions among various social groups in Gansu, once their price drops, it always causes prices to rise, and its impact on the livelihood of ordinary poor people is not insignificant, especially for those who run small businesses. Therefore, in terms of unifying the monetary policy, it is necessary to reorganize it, and in terms of the livelihood of ordinary people, it must be reorganized as soon as possible. However, once reorganized, the price of copper coins will inevitably rise, and copper coins from neighboring provinces will take advantage of the situation to enter. Where there is great profit, people will compete to go there, and even with strict laws and harsh punishments, it may not be possible to manage the aftermath well. This is why they hesitate all day long, thinking carefully but unable to find a solution. In short, currency is based on the nation as the unit, and it is not something that one province can do alone. Gansu Province only does its best within the possible range. As for unifying and standardizing it, so as to be on par with advanced and civilized countries, this is what they deeply hope from the central government. Fortunately, the Currency System Committee has already been established. Will there be a day when the complex, intricate, and bizarre problem of Chinese subsidiary coins will be resolved? They look forward to it. (Attached table omitted)

The general meeting of shareholders of the Bank of Communications passed new articles of association, stipulating the increase of industrial, commercial and merchant business such as granting false loans, and decided to hold a board meeting today. Details are recorded as follows:

Board Meeting Today

As for the chairman of the bank,

New Business Determined

Article 17 of the new articles of association of the Bank of Communications stipulates the types of business as follows: (1) Managing the underwriting or acceptance of corporate bonds issued by industrial companies; (2) Granting loans with reliable ancestral guarantees as collateral, and granting loans to industrial, commercial, and merchant companies; (3) Granting loans with industrial movable property as collateral, but the total amount of loans shall not exceed one-half of the paid-up capital; (4) Discounting or buying commercial bills and drafts with definite terms; (5) Receiving various deposits and safekeeping securities, bills, and all other valuables for others; (6) Trust and savings business; (7) Acting as an agent for collecting and resolving various payments; (8) Domestic and foreign remittances and cargo mortgage remittances; (9) Buying and selling securities, raw gold and silver, and currencies of various countries; (10) Warehousing, transportation, and insurance business; (11) Investing in the development of industry, but the amount of investment shall not exceed one-quarter of the share capital. According to the reporter of the New Voice News Agency, the old articles of association stipulated eight types of business in Article 16. Shanghai Silk Industry Bank Held Annual General Meeting of Shareholders Yesterday; Trust Department Added and Capital Increased by 800,000 Yuan; Xu Jilao and Chen Aishi Elected as Supervisors 95

The Shanghai Silk Industry Bank, located at No. 460 Hankou Road, has been established for four years. Yesterday at 2:00 p.m., the bank held its fourth annual general meeting of shareholders at the Bankers Association on Hong Kong Road. All directors and supervisors, including Wang Yansong, Yu Zuoting, Shen Qinqi, Wang Boyuan, Pei Yunqing, Chen Xiaodie, Chen Ziming, Xu Jilao, Gan Yongwen, and Lu Zhengbing, attended, as well as Manager Tian Xiangru, Deputy Manager Luo Qinghua, and shareholders Tang Shoumin, Liang Chenlan, Zheng Zenan, Chen Yongqing, Lu Baoyuan, Chuan Ruihe, Xu Shengyang, Ma Shaoquan, He Xialing, and more than 200 others, representing 6,750 shares. Chairman Wang Yansong first reported, saying, "Today, our bank is holding its fourth annual general meeting of shareholders. We are deeply honored by the presence of all shareholders. The business situation of our bank in the past year has been compiled into a report, which we ask you to review. Our bank has been handling businesses of a trust nature for a long time, and it has gradually become developed. Now, in order to achieve the effect of handling simple matters easily, we plan to establish a trust department from this year to be solely responsible for handling all trust businesses. However, the articles of association and the name of the bank should be appropriately revised. These two aspects have been drafted into proposals and await detailed discussion by all shareholders." Next, Director Wang reported on the business situation (recorded separately). Then, Supervisor Xu Jilao reported on the accounts in brief. Then, the agenda was discussed: (1) The bank plans to add a trust department and draft articles of association. Please pass the motion. Resolved: Passed. (2) The bank's business is expanding day by day. In order to increase its strength, it is proposed to increase the capital by 800,000 yuan. Please pass the motion. Resolved: Passed. (3) It is proposed to correct the name of the bank and change Article 1 of the bank's articles of association to "This bank is named Shanghai Silk Industry Bank Co., Ltd., abbreviated as Silk Industry Bank. Please discuss the motion. Resolved: Passed. (4) In the bank's savings department's articles of association, all instances of the words "savings office" are proposed to be changed to "department." Please pass the motion. Resolved: Passed. Finally, the vote

Election of Supervisors

The results of the ballot were: Xu Jilao received 4,278 votes, Cheng Yongwen received 4,276 votes, Chen Aishi received 3,817 votes, and Ge Shuqian received 3,761 votes. They were elected as supervisors of this session. Lu Zhengbing, who had the next most votes, received 507 votes. The meeting adjourned after a photo was taken. It was already past 5:00 p.m.

Business Report

The bank has been established for four years in an instant since its opening. At the beginning of its establishment, it coincided with the Shanghai Incident. The city's industry and commerce suffered a severe blow, and its vitality was depleted. By last year, the rural economy had already been declining. In addition, the implementation of the US silver policy and the depreciation of currencies in various countries caused China's finances to experience an unprecedented panic. There were financial storms in the silver and money industry, and there were those who were liquidated and went bankrupt. The severity of the situation was unprecedented in recent years. The silver and money industry is the hub of the re-industry. Since all industries are declining and depressed, finance is naturally stagnant and exhausted, which is a matter of course affecting the silver and money industry. The bank has always maintained a steady attitude, seeking progress in gradual progress and survival in panic. All business is based on prudence. Therefore, in the midst of the financial world's stormy seas, the bank is still at ease. This is naturally due to the faith of the society, but also to the efforts of the bank's shareholders to maintain and support it, making the bank's foundation solid. Now, the difficult pass has been overcome, and the business is getting better and better. This can be said to the shareholders in two aspects: one is the business situation of each branch, and the other is the various facilities that the bank is currently carrying out. Please allow me to briefly explain to the shareholders: (1) Business situation of each branch: The Hangzhou branch of the bank was established after the resolution of the fifth board of directors of the bank in the province. It has been reported to the previous general meeting of shareholders. After five months of preparation, it officially opened on April 16, 23 years. Last year, the actual business hours were only eight and a half months. After opening, Zhejiang Province encountered a drought unprecedented in 60 years, and the remnants of bandits in Anhui and Jiangxi repeatedly disturbed the border of Zhejiang. The general commerce of Hangzhou City became more and more depressed. Small and medium-sized shops often closed down. Even those with a long history and a good reputation were closed down and liquidated due to the weakness of the people's purchasing power and the stagnation of the accounts on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. The silk, tea, paper, and foil and other major products were also lifeless due to poor sales. In the general decline of industry and commerce, the Hangzhou branch has been progressing smoothly with the sincere cooperation of all sectors of the local community. In eight and a half months, the deposits received have reached about 800,000 yuan, and the total amount of receipts and payments has also exceeded 35.7 million yuan. The average daily balance of various deposits in the business department is 535,333 yuan. In the future, it will naturally carefully consider the business environment and the actual needs of various industries to properly handle each also. The Nanshi branch of the bank is a part of the former site of the Nanshi Chamber of Commerce, which was rented and repaired. It opened on March 21 last year. In the past year, it has received more than 160,000 yuan in various deposits. In the future, the number of people in Huhang who have a relationship with the bank will increase day by day. The Baxianqiao branch of the bank was established in mid-October of the 22nd year. It is the first branch established by the bank. The residents and shops in the area are very prosperous, and the business can be developed. However, since the Baxianqiao area is the center of concentration for various banks to establish branches, business competition is inevitable, and progress is difficult to achieve quickly. Various savings deposits have reached more than 130,000 yuan. The western district of the city has always been known as a residential area. Banking peers have successively set up branches in the Jing'an Temple Road area. At first, the bank did not have a suitable location, so it was still empty. Last November, the Western District Branch of the Four Banks Savings Association moved to a new house after its completion. The bank rented it because it was located between Jing'an Temple Road and Carter Road, which is convenient for transportation. It announced its opening on November 20. Although it has been a short time, the business is still smooth, and it is very promising. The bank has always paid close attention to the business of other places. Since the opening of the Hangzhou branch, it has made every effort to promote the business in Zhejiang Province. Shaoxing is the old capital of eastern Zhejiang, and its commerce has always been prosperous. In the past ten years, wars and disasters have continued in various provinces, rural areas have gone bankrupt, and people have no means of livelihood. Shaoxing is located in the east of Zhejiang, far from the center, and there are few soldiers. Residents have settled in their respective industries, producing silk and wine, which are sold at home and abroad. The amount is quite large, and the folk customs are simple, hardworking, and patient, which is a feature. Therefore, in this time of worldwide recession, the people are generally rich. The only rich county is Shaoxing. Therefore, the bank decided to set up a branch there and found a site in Shuicheng Lane. The sixth meeting of the second board of directors decided to hire Xu Shengyang as manager. It opened on March 2, 2016. Although the business is not yet a month, it has gained considerable credibility, and the future outlook can be predicted. (2) Facilities under construction: The bank has been handling businesses of a trust nature for a long time, and it has gradually become developed, such as the securities department's buying and selling securities on behalf of customers, the warehouse department's depositing goods, the safe deposit box department's renting safe deposit boxes, and the real estate department's renting houses. In addition, it has signed an insurance special agreement with Tianyi Insurance Company to manage insurance on behalf of customers, etc. These are all aspects of the development of the wood industry. It is now planned to establish a trust department to be solely responsible for handling all trust businesses, so as to achieve the effect of managing simple matters easily. Furthermore, the bank is aware that the market in the Hongkou area is gradually becoming prosperous, and is currently planning to set up a Hongkou branch to assist in the arms and fingers. In addition to working hard to promote various businesses, the bank has never forgotten to run social undertakings. Recently, in view of the increasingly large and complex economic organizations, laws, and personnel in the society, a general department has been specially created to provide consultation and research for all sectors. The scope of this consultation is temporarily divided into (1) academics, (2) economics, (3) law, and (4) personnel, and experts are invited to serve as special contracted instructors. At the same time, a monthly publication, tentatively named "Silk Weaving," will be published to selectively disclose the answers to various consultations and other valuable works. All of these facilities are intended to serve the society. In short, "seeking credit with service" and "seeking pure profit with credit" are the bank's only creeds. In the future, it will naturally strive to live up to the elegant expectations of all shareholders.
