Shen Bao Medical Weekly

The Lecithin Smoking Cessation Problem (Lipid-Like Substance Smoking Cessation Problem) (2) 198

— Pang Jingzhou

How did the lecithin smoking cessation method come into being?

Mr. Ma Wenzhao has already explained the principles and process of lecithin smoking cessation as described above. Since then, it has naturally been adopted by smoking cessation hospitals in Nanjing. At the same time, Mr. Ma also conducted a third study on cell metamorphosis to answer questions such as whether the lipid-like substances required by the Golgi apparatus of various cells are related to the increase in platelets and how leukocytes transport lipid-like substances. He still used white mice for experiments, and the main results are as follows:

(A) Morphine may stimulate red blood cells to produce a large number of platelets, as mentioned above, and the important component of platelets is lipid-like substances.

(B) During the withdrawal period, after the increase in platelets, the lipid-like substances in leukocytes also increase, and platelets are found inside anuclear leukocytes. The number of leukocytes in blood vessels greatly decreases, while the number of leukocytes in various organs greatly increases. From this, it is known that leukocytes contain a large number of lipid-like substances or platelets in the bloodstream, transporting them to various organs to supply the remodeling of the Golgi apparatus.

(C) During the craving period, the number of platelets greatly decreases, and leukocytes have nothing to absorb. Therefore, it is found that many are stagnant in the blood vessels, seemingly waiting to absorb lipid-like substances. At the same time, leukocytes in various organs greatly decrease, and the Golgi apparatus also decreases, or even disappears.

(D) After feeding lecithin, leukocytes immediately absorb this lipid-like substance from the intestinal wall to meet needs, without the need for red blood cells to produce a large number of platelets. Therefore, the number of leukocytes retained in the blood vessels is found to decrease, while the number in organs greatly increases again.

The report of this study is detailed in the "Chinese Journal of Physiology," Volume 7, Issue 4, pages 287-342, 1933, entitled "Changes in Leukocytes During Long-Term Morphine Addiction and Treatment in White Mice."

Last year, during the Far Eastern Tropical Medicine Conference in Nanjing, Mr. Ma and two physicians from the Nanjing Municipal Smoking Cessation Hospital jointly published a paper in the proceedings of the conference, entitled "A Comfortable and Spontaneous Cure of Opium Habit by Means of a Lecithin Diet."

According to this clinical experimental report, taking a large amount of lecithin has the possibility of stopping smoking immediately, allowing smokers to quit themselves. It also has eight major effects: mental pleasure, weight gain, smooth bowel movements, stable sleep, strong appetite, rapid reduction of addiction, no withdrawal symptoms, and natural reduction of smoking. From the above two articles, it can be known that researchers were quite satisfied with lecithin as of last year. Therefore, the Ministry of Health sold "Xinsheng Brand Lecithin" products in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang areas last winter. The initial intention of the Ministry of Health was also to promote and popularize smoking cessation. Therefore, the product name was even given the name "Xinsheng" (新生), meaning it aligns with the New Life Movement. However, several steps were missing in the distribution process, so the usage method did not fully comply with the conditions of Mr. Ma's experiments, resulting in the current market being filled with chaotic rumors and rambling criticisms. The sources are described separately as follows:

(A) According to the experiments conducted by Mr. Ma et al. in the municipal hospital, forty drug offenders sent by the court were used as the standard, which is different from ordinary smokers in terms of environment and mentality.

(B) The experiments conducted by Mr. Ma et al. were conducted in a hospital setting. The smoking cessation procedures and the method of taking lecithin were all under the control of physicians, and the process was examined in detail. At the same time, other drugs were used to treat the drug offenders.

(C) Mr. Ma et al. originally stated that the effectiveness of this smoking cessation method is still based on his cellular studies and does not encompass all effects of opium, which can be relieved by lecithin.

(D) In the conclusion of the paper, Mr. Ma et al. hoped that other medical cases and hospitals would conduct expanded experiments and requested colleagues to study and criticize (To be continued)

Three-Year Health Implementation Plan of Nanjing Municipal Baguazhou Farmers' Education Center (Continued) 199

— Hua Xinren

Second item: Farmers' Health Care

Rural health work should prioritize treatment first. Once the people have faith in "new medicine," all long-standing problems can be easily solved. The design of this center for this issue is as follows:

(1) Disease Treatment: Outpatient work, mobile treatment, referrals

(2) Health Education: The time spent waiting for consultation is used by the staff of this office.

A. Explain the phenomena and causes of diseases

B. Explain the relationship between disease and people and prevention methods

C. Health problem consultation and answers

(3) Home Visits: A. Patients who have come to the clinic and have special circumstances

B. Impart hygiene knowledge and provide home care

C. Isolation of infectious diseases and disinfection of equipment

D. Connect with farmers' feelings

(4) Plague Prevention Work: A. Fully cooperate with the Nanjing Anti-Malaria Committee

B. Train farmers to fill ditches and polluted water

C. Investigate the number of malaria patients

D. Divide the island and designate it as a medication area

(5) Maternal and Child Health: There is no new method of midwifery on the island, and special attention should be paid to maternal and child health. The implementation plan for this work is as follows:

A. Women's Class: The center's midwife teaches maternal and child health knowledge

B. Family Meetings: Gather housewives from each family together for training in one organization so that they can solve common issues that are close to them, and then be influenced by interest.

B. Training and Registration of Midwives: Management of old-fashioned midwives

D. Midwifery Work: Those who have come to the center for prenatal checkups will receive free midwifery services and postnatal visits.

E. Infant Mortality Investigation: The township office reports to the center, and the center conducts infant mortality investigations during diagnosis and treatment.

(6) Others: Matters related to farmers' health care

Third item: Environmental Sanitation

The quality of environmental sanitation is related to overall health. The occurrence and spread of diseases are closely related to the environment. The points that need to be addressed in terms of environmental sanitation on the island are:

A. Digging Wells: Disinfect the wells daily

B. Constructing Public Toilets: A good method for dealing with indiscriminate defecation. The style should adopt the Javanese toilet.

C. Garbage Disposal: Set up trash cans and collect them at designated times

D. Other Management: Teahouses, restaurants, bathhouses, vegetable markets, barber shops, etc.

Fourth item: Special Work.

A. Train health care workers to complete the township autonomous health care system.

Given the size of the island and the number of people, the distribution of the staff in this office is particularly difficult. If farmers with some knowledge within the island can be given general health training and organization, this problem can be avoided and the great effect of public autonomy can be achieved. It is planned to select outstanding individuals from the graduates of the island's adult class, the children's class, and the women's class, and organize and train them in this office. The method will be detailed in another article.

B. Vital Statistics: Concluded by this office in conjunction with the township office.

Those who manage rural hygiene should integrate education, agriculture, and hygiene into one, which means combining agriculture, education, and hygiene into one, dividing labor and cooperating so that the work is not difficult.

We firmly believe that hygiene is particularly important in the method of rescuing rural areas, because rural areas are the foundation of society, and farmers account for 85% of our country's population. Therefore, if we want to revitalize our nation and save the declining phenomenon, we must first start with farmers' hygiene.

If we want to build a new China and make our people wash away the shame of being the sick men of East Asia, there is no other way than rural hygiene.

Since Xinren first entered rural work, he has had great ambitions for reviving the health of farmers. Because he feels that if he wants to implement rural health work, he should first educate the public about hygiene. Therefore, he drafted the above plan. He dared not publish it to readers before, but "throwing a brick to attract jade" has been a clear motto since ancient times. Moreover, "a rustic's offering of sunshine should not be criticized by gentlemen." Therefore, he hopes to receive guidance from experts from all walks of life.

A Brief History of School Oral Hygiene in Various Countries (3) 200

— Situ Xue

There are many types of school dental management methods in the United States, which can be roughly divided into state-run, city-run, social organizations, or foundation-run. As for school dental facilities, the Forsyth Children's Dental Clinic in Boston and the Rochester Dental Hospital in Rochester City are the greatest and most ideal representatives of central treatment centers. Other cities also have central treatment facilities. The city of Bridgeport is located in the municipal hall, and simple dental clinics are also set up in more than 30 primary schools in the city. In general, they are mostly managed by the Bureau of Education, the Bureau of Health, the Red Cross, and the Tuberculosis Prevention Association.

The school dental facilities in the metropolis are managed as described above. As for the countryside, because it is not easy to set up a central treatment center, mobile dental treatment teams are organized. These mobile teams also adopt various methods. The simple ones only carry folding chairs and hand-held equipment for home visits. In remote areas, cars or carriages are used to set up a simple treatment room inside for mobile home visits, which is very convenient.

Oral Hygiene Movement in France

Oral hygiene facilities in France began on March 23, 1908. According to the decree promulgated by the Bureau of Social Education, all students in primary schools and normal schools must undergo oral examinations and treatment. After the promulgation of this decree, two dentists were appointed to be responsible for the task of examination and treatment. Oral examinations were carried out twice a year, and the oral condition of the examinees was filled in the examination certificate and sent to their parents. However, whether to treat or not was up to them. At that time, there were no school treatment facilities, so those who wanted to be treated mostly went to private dental hospitals that they agreed with for treatment. However, the treating doctor was not restricted by the examining doctor, and the examining doctor only examined the oral condition of the students.

Before the promulgation of this decree, the dental community in France had a strong enthusiasm for promoting the oral hygiene movement, but because the education authorities were indifferent, its development was not as advanced as in England, the United States, and Germany. At that time, little attention was paid to the oral hygiene of primary school children, but students above middle school occasionally received it. In 1908, after the promulgation of this decree, a clause on teeth was added to the prescribed duties of school doctors, ordering school doctors to fill in a detailed record of the oral condition of each student. According to the law, students who will be employed in the education sector or normal schools in the future must undergo two oral examinations a year and be advised to receive treatment. At that time, that was all that was done for oral hygiene, and there was really no contribution. Two years later, middle schools other than normal schools gradually stipulated examinations. As for primary school children, there are still no legal regulations. It was not until the House of Commons put forward a bill to conduct oral examinations for primary school children that it was gradually realized.

Page 16

In 1912, the city of Nice and others began to establish municipal school dental clinics, and charitable organizations, dental medical associations, dental schools, etc. in Paris and other major cities also established them one after another to provide voluntary services.

The French Oral Hygiene Association was founded in 1911. Its purpose is (1) to make the public aware of the importance of oral hygiene, which is not only important for maintaining healthy teeth, but also important for personal physical health, and is also governed by the development of the race. (2) To popularize oral hygiene education to the public through lectures, lantern slides, etc. (3) To implement oral examinations and treatment in schools, military units, and various charitable organizations. The members of this dental hygiene association are not only dentists, but also include knowledge classes such as congressmen, journalists, and educators to work together for development, so oral hygiene in France is progressing day by day.

The Importance of Vitamins to Life (1) 201

— Zhong Zhihe

Vitamins, also known as vitamin elements, are a type of organic substance found in various foods. They were first discovered by Mr. Kasimir Funk twenty-two years ago. Since then, doctors all over the world have studied them carefully and clarified their principles, and only then did they realize that they are necessary elements in the human body's metabolism! Once there is a lack or absence of this type of substance, it is easy to cause various diseases of vitamin deficiency. The importance of vitamins to life is indeed great.

However, many of our compatriots often do not ask for medical knowledge, do not understand how vitamins are classified, and what their functions are, and often buy vitamins as tonics. This is like sailing in the dark without a compass, blindly without knowing where to go. As a result, they only waste money and gain nothing, which is really regrettable.

I, a member of the medical community, do not want my compatriots to fall into this fog any longer, so I wrote this article to tell my compatriots, so that they will have a clear understanding of the value of vitamins in the future, so that they can be used properly and effectively. I hope my compatriots will not neglect it. Here, I will describe vitamins in detail, which I believe my compatriots will be happy to read to the end.

Vitamin A

May also be called anti-ophthalmic and anti-infective vitamin

Effects on the human body

(1) Prevents infectious diseases, especially in the eyes and respiratory system.

(2) Promotes growth and longevity;

(3) Maintains health and physical strength

(4) Promotes appetite and digestion

(5) It has an important effect on ordinary reproduction, lactation, and childhood feeding.

(6) It has the effect of increasing resistance to puerperal sepsis. Pregnant women taking it can increase resistance and make it less susceptible to infection after childbirth.

(7) It is said to have considerable function for pneumonia

(8) Increases the activity of bone marrow

(9) Maintains the integrity of epithelial tissue and can prevent tissue cells from developing diseases, such as in the respiratory system, nourishing tract, kidneys, pelvic bones, bladder, vas deferens, prostate, eyes, and ductless glands.

Results of deficiency or absence

(1) Decreased resistance to bacterial infectious diseases or changes in the immune properties in the blood.

(2) Growth and development are hindered and delayed

(3) Susceptible to the following infectious diseases——

(A) Lymph glands at the base of the tongue are prone to abscesses

(B) Sinuses are prone to suppuration, and ears are prone to otitis media

(C) Eyes are prone to night blindness and xerophthalmia

(D) Tear glands lose their ability to produce tears

(E) Salivary glands, lymph glands, lungs, nose, and skin are all susceptible to infection

(F) Kidneys, ureters, and bladder are susceptible to infection and are prone to calculi

(G) Alimentary Canal is prone to infection

(4) Diarrhea

(5) Physical weakness

(6) Loss of appetite and indigestion

(7) Infertility due to failure of the egg production process

(8) Prone to Pernicious Anemia

(9) Secretory epithelium often becomes keratinized

Vitamin B1

Also known as antineuritic and antiberiberi vitamin. Effects on the human body

(1) Increases appetite and aids digestion

(2) Promotes metabolism and promotes growth

(3) Protects the body from nervous system diseases (such as beriberi and Polyneutis

(4) A necessary product for promoting infant growth during breastfeeding by the mother

(5) Increases the tension of digestive system muscles

Results of deficiency or absence

(1) Decreased or loss of appetite

(2) Digestion process is disturbed, secretion of digestive juices is reduced, peristalsis of the gastrointestinal tract is reduced and lacks tension.

(3) Infant growth is affected due to lack of this substance in the mother during breastfeeding

(4) Infertility due to cessation of the courtship period

(5) Anhydiemia

(6) Weight loss, sharp decline in physical strength, and even gastrointestinal damage

(7) Body temperature is below normal

(8) Fatigue

(9) Develop beriberi or polyneuritis and exhibit the following phenomena!

(A) Loss of coordinated muscle movement

(B) Limbs gradually become paralyzed

(C) Nourishing tract is disturbed, indigestion, constipation, colitis

(D) Emaciation

(10) Tongue atrophy, glossitis

Or call it Antiscorbunc Vitamin

Pain Relief in Medicine (11) 202

— Li Yu

Even normal menstruation can have some pain, but not unbearable pain. What is discussed here is abnormal pain. One treatment for menstrual pain is to use heat, such as applying a hot, moist compress or drinking hot beverages. Secondly, sedatives and pain relievers can be used. Regular bowel movements and practicing personal hygiene can also reduce menstrual pain. Sometimes, surgical correction of the uterine position is necessary.

Back Pain (Lumbago)

Back pain is not a rare ailment. You can see large advertisements for back pain remedies in newspapers. A large portion of plaster sales relies on customers with back pain. Common treatments for back pain are often not aligned with the pathology, so they are often futile. What's going on? Back pain is a very complex problem. Years of research have revealed no fewer than one hundred and twenty causes of back pain. If all types of back pain are treated the same way, good results cannot be expected. Due to space limitations, I cannot describe all the causes of back pain one by one. Here is a brief description of the most important causes: Now, let's talk from the outside in; inflammation of the back muscles can cause back pain. This inflammation often comes from chronic inflammation of the mouth, nose, and throat. From the muscles further inward, there are bones, the spine, and the pelvis; problems with these can also cause back pain. Spinal tuberculosis and common inflammation are also causes of back pain. The spine is made up of more than twenty movable small vertebral segments, and the lower end forms a slightly movable joint with the pelvis. These vertebral segments bear the weight of the upper body, move constantly, and are easily injured accidentally; for example, during pregnancy and childbirth. Women who have many children have more back pain. If the legs are of unequal length or the hip joint is misaligned, causing one side of the spine to bear more weight than the other, it can also cause back pain. Abscesses on the inner surface of the spine or outside the kidney are also commonly mistaken for back pain.

For women, the most common cause of back pain is problems with the organs in the pelvis. For example, endometritis, uterine malposition, oophoritis, salpingitis, pelvic abscesses, uterine tumors, ovarian tumors, etc. Therefore, to treat back pain in women, you must first understand this pathology. If you have back pain and just stick a few plasters on your back, isn't that futile?

Kidney (commonly known as the waist) problems are also a cause of back pain; for example, nephritis, kidney stones, kidney tuberculosis, kidney tumors, wandering kidney, etc. Secondly, people who are particularly obese in the abdomen often have back pain. Tertiary syphilis growing on the spine can also cause back pain.

From this, it can be seen that treating back pain is not a simple matter. Doctors who treat back pain must have sufficient internal medicine knowledge, and they must also be proficient in surgery, orthopedics, gynecology, etc. If patients have medical knowledge, they will not be easily fooled.

There are several standards for treating back pain that must be paid attention to. Don't just stick plasters or take pills when you have back pain. First, you need to know if the spine, vertebral joints, or pelvic joints are inflamed. If it is determined that the above is the cause, treatment requires resting the body, using heat, support, and removing the root cause. If it is bone tuberculosis, it must be treated according to the methods for treating bone tuberculosis. Second, women with back pain must pay attention to uterine disease, such as tumors or problems in the pelvis, which cannot be solved by applying plasters or taking kidney pills. Surgery or gynecological methods must be used to remove the problem before the back pain can be cured.

Third, special attention should be paid to kidney disease. Common people often mistake any back pain for "kidney" disease. Common people often think that pain in the lower back is caused by kidney disease. In fact, the kidneys are in the upper part of the waist, not the lower part. Kidney problems are certainly a cause of back pain, but not all back pain is caused by kidney disease. There are several types of kidney disease that cause back pain, such as kidney stones and kidney tuberculosis, which cannot be resolved with pills. Even common nephritis is not as simple to treat as advertised.

Secondly, people who are particularly obese should reduce the burden on their waist. People with legs of unequal length should wear shoes with different heel heights to balance the waist.

Acute Epididymitis

People with gonorrhea often develop epididymitis, the cause of which is that gonococci reach the epididymis through the vas deferens from the urethra, causing acute inflammation. At the same time, the testicles are also swollen. Acute epididymitis and orchitis are very painful conditions. If some basic principles are understood, epididymitis can be prevented, and the pain of epididymitis and orchitis can be reduced. Preventing this disease is not

Preventing this disease is not particularly difficult; it can be done as long as the pathology is understood. First, people with gonorrhea must use medication to wash the urethra or perform any kind of surgery gently. Second, do not injure the testicles. Third, people with gonorrhea, even if the testicles have no problems, must always wear a scrotal support (or elastic support). Although this cannot absolutely prevent epididymitis and orchitis, it can prevent eight or nine out of ten cases.

To stop the pain of acute epididymitis and orchitis, the most important thing is not narcotics or pain relievers. The most important things are: (1) Bed rest. (2) Lift up the swollen and painful scrotum, preferably so that it cannot move at all; a support made of adhesive tape is best. (3) Local heat or cold can reduce pain (cold is better than heat). Analgesic paste also has some benefit. (4) Taking or injecting painkillers once to several times is also very reasonable.

Heart Pain

Before we talk about heart pain, let's first talk about the location of the heart. If we don't know where the heart is, we can't easily know what heart pain is. As the saying goes, "Put your conscience in the middle." Speaking of which, the conscience should be in the middle, but the heart is not in the middle of the chest. The location of the heart is: in front of the chest, reaching the third costal cartilage, i.e., the second intercostal space below. Below it reaches the middle seventh costal cartilage, and left and right it reaches the fifth intercostal space. The lower part of the heart on the left side is about three and a half inches from the midline, one and a half inches inside the left nipple. The right side is about two inches from the midline, so the position of the heart is in the middle of the chest, slightly to the left, and not in the very center.

Knowing the position of the heart makes it easier to know whether the pain is heart pain when there is heart pain. Heart pain is treated for heart pain, and the results are good. If it is not heart pain and is treated as heart pain, there will certainly be no good results.

To understand heart pain, you must also understand the structure and pathology of the heart. Here is a brief description: The outside of the heart has two layers of double-folded thin membrane that completely enclose the heart; this membrane is called the pericardium. The envelope is sometimes inflamed and is called pericarditis. This kind of heart pain is often in the chest in front of the heart. The pain is sometimes like a knife stabbing, sometimes dull. Sometimes this pain also reflects to the abdomen. Do not mistake it for abdominal disease.

Since the pericardium is double-layered, sometimes pericarditis produces fluid between these two layers, making the patient feel chest tightness and pain. To stop this pain, this liquid must be extracted and rested.

Inside the pericardium is the heart muscle. Inflammation of the heart muscle is called myocarditis. Myocarditis often has heart pain. Chronic myocarditis is often chronic pain. This pain often starts when exerting force or when the heart is stimulated. The pain is in the upper part of the sternum, or in the upper part of the left chest, or in the chest in front of the heart, or reflects to the left shoulder, left arm, left hand, or the corner of the left lower jaw. Rarely does it reflect to the right side of the body. Myocarditis pain can be mild or severe; mild pain is just a feeling of chest tightness, while severe pain is unbearable, as if the heart is being squeezed in a blacksmith's screw clamp and twisted tight. At the same time, the chest feels constricted, and there is a sense of impending death. The pain often occurs after meals, probably because after meals, more blood gathers in the stomach and intestines, and the heart muscle feels anemic. Patients rarely experience pain at rest or during sleep, except in the late stages of myocarditis. In mild cases, there are often several months of no recurrence after recovery, while in severe cases, the number of pains is more frequent, and the periods without pain are less frequent. When the pain comes, the patient must immediately stop moving, and the pain usually passes within a few minutes. Sometimes the pain reaches its peak, and the patient dies immediately. Some die after the heart has been in pain for a long time and is exhausted.

To stop this kind of heart pain, inhaling amyl nitrite when the pain comes can immediately stop the pain. But the fundamental treatment still requires removing the root cause and resting. Remove the root cause, for example, radically treating rheumatic pain, local root causes, syphilis (tertiary syphilis), high blood pressure, nephritis, and other diseases.

A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis (48) 203

— Hu Jiayan

Chapter 10 The Prognosis of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

The patient's age is also very related to the prognosis. Infants under one or two years old are the most dangerous, and almost all are incurable; however, the number of cases of this disease is actually less than that of adults. Adolescents who have just passed puberty (over sixteen years old) are also particularly dangerous. From then until about thirty years old, they are all within the scope of the danger period. From thirty-five to over fifty years old, most of this disease is chronic, and the prognosis is relatively good. But above fifty-four or five years old, due to the consumption of physical strength, this disease becomes malignant again, and the result often endangers life, which is called senile tuberculosis. In those over three years old and under puberty, the prognosis of this disease is generally better.

The patient's personality is also different from person to person, each with its own characteristics; the result will also affect the disease itself. Some people are extremely sensitive; they have always held a terrifying attitude towards this disease; they do not know that the severity of this disease varies greatly. For example, the early infiltration type can mostly be cured if treated properly; but because the patient is too timid and nervous, the impact on the future is great. Some people have a very strong will, and everywhere they hold the attitude that man will conquer nature, thinking that there is nothing to worry about. But in serious times, like high fever, they should absolutely rest, and cavities should be specially treated, etc., he will sometimes turn a deaf ear; the result will inevitably become worse!

Whether the patient's treatment plan is appropriate? And whether long-term recuperation is carried out? There is a big difference in the situation for the prognosis. We can boldly say that the sooner the proper treatment, the greater the hope for the future. As for the suitability of living in a place for health, the appropriateness of nutrition, and the patient's environment, etc.: all have a great relationship with the patient's future, and must not be regarded as a mere formality.

Finally, the patient's economic situation has absolute authority over the patient's future. Many cases of this disease are not extremely bad at first, but abandoning work and long-term treatment are actually impossible for the patient; the result is that they become worse day by day, leading to incurable; this kind of example is probably countless. But this is the problem of the entire country and society, and of course it cannot be individually undertaken by practicing physicians and private hospitals! (End of this chapter)

Common Sense of Hygiene for the Ears, Nose, Throat, and Eyes 204

— Tang Renjin

(44) Tinnitus

Our ear organs. When there are sound wave vibrations from the outside world. They can immediately generate hearing through the sound-receiving function. If there are no sound wave vibrations from the outside world. Then hearing will not occur, which is a natural principle. But sometimes. There are no sound wave vibrations from the outside world. One can indeed hear a kind of sound oneself. This is what is called tinnitus. People in general believe that tinnitus is a sign of physical weakness and qi deficiency. This kind of explanation. Is rather vague. If we speak clearly from the perspective of otology. Tinnitus is actually a kind of auditory sensation that comes from abnormal excitation of the auditory nerve. This auditory sensation is only felt by oneself. Others do not feel it. Therefore, tinnitus is also called subjective hearing. Tinnitus often occurs with diseases of the auditory organs. For example, in acute catarrhal otitis media, chronic catarrhal otitis media, acute suppurative otitis media, chronic suppurative otitis media, otosclerosis, labyrinthine anemia, labyrinthine hyperemia, various poisonings, and inner ear inflammation, etc. Tinnitus is often a necessary symptom. The pitch, type, strength, duration, and pain of tinnitus are all different. Now I will briefly describe them as follows.

(1) Pitch of tinnitus The pitch of tinnitus is ever-changing. There are low, high, harmonious, disharmonious, clear, and mixed sounds, etc.

(2) Types of tinnitus The sound characteristics of tinnitus can often be distinguished as buzzing, cicada chirping, insect chirping, wind sound, bell sound, flute sound, water bubble sound, boiling water sound, wave sound, and ringing, etc.

(3) Strength of tinnitus When in a happy mood, refreshed, sunny weather, moderate labor, and normal menstruation, etc. The degree of tinnitus is often weak. When angry, upset, in a bad mood, mentally exhausted, in changing weather, overworked, abnormal menstruation, reproductive organ disorders, and pregnancy, etc. The degree of tinnitus is often strong.

(4) Duration of tinnitus There are three types of tinnitus duration. Namely, paroxysmal, intermittent, and continuous. Among them, continuous tinnitus has a relatively poor prognosis.

(5) Pain of tinnitus The pain of tinnitus. First, it hinders hearing. Second, it easily causes annoyance. Third, it is mistaken for sound. When the degree of tinnitus is severe. It can often prevent people from engaging in work. Or hinder sleep. Or even be unable to endure the pain and commit suicide.

Firecrackers or Bombs? 205

— Long

A Reuters dispatch from London on the 20th stated that Germany's letter of protest against the League of Nations resolution has been simultaneously submitted to the fourteen countries of the League of Nations Council. Its wording is far from what foreign sources predicted. Government officials said, "This is not a bomb, but a firecracker." The explosive power of firecrackers and bombs naturally has a difference as vast as the sky and the earth. Is Germany's letter of protest really a firecracker or a bomb? It is worth discussing.

In everything, onlookers are clear, and those involved are confused. Those involved exhaust their scheming, engage in infighting, and do their best to manipulate and operate. However, onlookers consider it unworthy of a smile. The League of Nations resolution, in the eyes of the League of Nations, is naturally a huge bomb thrown at Germany. However, in the eyes of the Germans, it is nothing more than a firecracker. Although we have not seen the original text of Germany's letter of protest, judging from the London dispatch, the content of the note is a straightforward letter of protest against the League of Nations resolution. Although its wording is strong, it is restrained. Judging from these few words, it is enough to see that Germany's letter of protest is actually a bomb, not comparable to the firecrackers set off at temple fairs.

In Germany's opinion, you fourteen countries can pass resolutions as you please, but we Germany will never recognize them. See what else you can do? There is no need to say more. In this way, the League of Nations resolution is equivalent to waste paper, and the seriousness of its letter of protest can be generally seen. However, the British are calm and wave their feather fans lightly, saying: "This is a firecracker, not a bomb." There are originally unavoidable difficulties in it. The British attitude towards Germany's situation is different from that of France and Italy. On the one hand, Britain is a member of the League of Nations, and on the other hand, it is willing to be a mediator and does not want to join the vortex. Once the meeting starts, it cannot stay out of it and has to support the resolution (Britain is also one of the signatory countries of Versailles). In this way, Britain really has a difficult situation of pleasing both sides. Britain really has unspeakable pain, and the reason is here.

Therefore, although Germany firmly opposes the League of Nations resolution, Britain can only deal with it with a calm attitude and cannot help but say a few sarcastic remarks. On the one hand, as a country of the League of Nations resolution, if it overemphasizes Germany's protest, not only will its own face not look good, but it will also not be able to turn around. On the other hand, Britain is willing to be a mediator and does not want both parties to break down. If there is an opportunity for mediation, the British are still willing to come out to mediate. Therefore, in any tense atmosphere, they must say something to ease it. This is in the British psyche, they cannot but harbor such a wish, as a basis for changing course later.

But turning back to look at Germany's attitude, what is it like? A dispatch from Berlin on the 20th stated that for Hitler's birthday, troops were reviewed and power was displayed. At the same time, the letter of protest against the League of Nations was announced, and the important significance of the government's decision to reorganize its armed forces was reiterated. Broadcasting to various countries, the civil servants' union contributed one million marks to present to the leader, as the corner of the German people's physical training. Judging from this point, is Germany's letter of protest really a firecracker? Or a bomb? What exactly is it?

Spring Cold 206

— Yafei

Since the beginning of spring this year, there have not been many clear days, but there has also been very little rain. The peach blossom water in March did not flow down as people imagined. However, the overcast sky all day long, without seeing a few full suns, is indeed the reality.

"Ah! God is simply going to take the lives of poor people. Last year, it was so dry and satisfying for a year, but this year it is such a face again. The weather is overcast, and even the weather in April is not so cold. It is said that the spring harvest will be greatly discounted, and I am afraid that the flowers and fruits on the trees and the future paddy fields will also be affected by it!"

Recently, Little Tiger Cai Shun often sighed, cursing the sky to himself, resenting the sky, and complaining that God was deliberately going against him. In fact, he didn't know that every farmer was not in the same fate as him, struggling under the oppression of famine and terror! After eating today, I don't know where tomorrow will be. After tomorrow, I don't know how the day after tomorrow will go on? Sometimes, perhaps, even today cannot be survived. Such a miserable situation can be easily seen at any time and anywhere in every rural area today.

Little Tiger Cai Shun's family has eleven mouths to feed, and only he and his eldest son, A Gen, can work. In previous years, in addition to farming, they also had a sideline—tying paper houses—冥屋 (miniature paper house burned at funerals), which earned at most about two hundred yuan a year. But now, where would there be any spare money to transcend ancestors and burn paper houses?

For three years, he has not been able to harvest flowers and fruits, and the fields have been planted in vain, and no one has asked him to tie paper houses anymore. Thus, his entire source of life has been completely dried up!

A few loads of grain were harvested the year before last. After paying off the grain and rent, there was only a limited amount left. They drank bean porridge for every meal, barely making it to last spring before it was gone. Last year, the fields were cracked from the drought, and the newly transplanted seedlings all withered and died. There has been no income for a full year until now: living by pawning, selling, and borrowing. Now, everything that can be pawned has been pawned, all the borrowing has been exhausted, and even if there is something to buy, no one wants it. This kind of life is really suffering for Little Tiger Cai Shun! Last year, he often comforted himself, thinking: "After a great famine, there will be a great harvest!" So he fully expected this year to be a year of great harvest, which could compensate for last year's poor harvest, and perhaps some of the borrowed money could be paid back, and some of the pawned items could be redeemed. Unexpectedly, the first shot of this year's spring harvest shattered his dream. The autumn harvest is still a very slim hope!

Because Little Tiger Cai Shun had too many mouths to feed, he managed to entrust someone to recommend his fourteen-year-old second son to a preserved goods store to work as an apprentice, and hastily married his seventeen-year-old daughter to her fiancé's family, while sending his twelve-year-old youngest daughter to a small fishing boat to be a child bride. In this way, three mouths were reduced on his shoulders. However, there are still eight people to feed, and eight people are not easy to deal with after all! Therefore, he often felt that he was in danger of being swallowed:

"Alas! The harvest is so poor, and there are so many mouths to feed. One day I will be swallowed by them, alas! One day..."

"Spring cold freezes old yellow cattle!" Besides worrying and cursing about the gray sky every day, what else can he do?

The Birth of a Home 207

— Cheng Quan

We two have already reached the borderline of middle age, and we both understand: we are no longer children who can enter paradise, nor are we suited to regard the friendship and love between boys and girls built on the foundation of real life as a poetic game to admire and yearn for; as older adults, why are we always lingering on the fringes of life without settling down? Moreover, this is not a one-time or two-time thing: some acquaintances all look at us with puzzled thoughts: "You're not wanderers, you should have a home." Indeed, what they say is absolutely right, even we ourselves have thought that way long ago: we should have a home! Isn't it so? Even ants have their own lovely little nests, why should people be born into wandering and then have to endlessly continue this frightening eternal wandering? — This is not an easy life.

It is a fact; we two are gradually leaving the joyful paradise of youth, and on the other hand, we experience a slight sense of emptiness from the perspective of middle age: understanding that this is the time to face life with a serious face, we feel afraid and lonely; then we think that two people who have come through rosy love affairs must begin to squeeze together; that is to say, we must have our own little nest.

Both of us have that kind of feeling and need, so we think: even if our strength is as weak as ants, ants are also very brave in using their own labor to build their own small shelter. So, we took two still childish hearts, and with the patience and labor of ants, fearless, without worry, and without shrinking back, we began to choose "to use our own labor to create a lovely little home" as the goal of our lives in this lonely and desolate world, and walked the same path that everyone must go through from childhood to middle age.

Perhaps the thing called "home" is somewhat frightening? Yes, no one can deny this. However, life itself is just a kind of temptation, a kind of longing. When the charming shadow of a comfortable home begins to shine incessantly on the borderline of middle age, people forget everything, people desperately go for her, get her, forgetting the danger, and forgetting the fear!

Similarly, for the sake of home, for the sake of our own home, we have to start a period of frightening labor, we two need strength in the treacherous waves of life; first of all, for the difficult material foundation, we have to desperately increase our respective labor, even voluntarily increasing work to more than twelve hours a day.

Page 18

We have also worked hard to endure unspeakable long periods of separation, but these were all endured with the greatest possible patience, and what followed were the stumbling blocks of the old social system, so, in order to remove, resist, and crush them, strength and courage became necessary again. We two were weak in our youth; but even if we are weak, what does it matter? People walk along their own path, work, and sweat, so, we gradually won the possibility of being together, had a place to live, had furniture that increased from one piece to two pieces, had a kind of mood suitable for two young people to work together, and had a home.

A home was born! But a kind of uncomfortable terror that starts from life's actions was also born. The days are endlessly long, but life is endlessly vague; yet, we are "people with a home" now.

Like a dying snail wandering at the foot of the wall: carrying its shell, I begin to feel its weight, and I am afraid.

Fishing Season 208

— Shi Feng

The residents of Wengjiazhai live by fishing. Every spring and autumn are the seasons when fish are most abundant. Wengjia Pond is an official river. As long as one does not encroach on anyone's dam (although the dams are also privately built), no one dares to interfere with net fishing on one's own fish dam all day long. But the dozens of fishermen there are all law-abiding, and they entrust their lives to this pond. When it is the spawning season, no one is seen casting nets to fish on each dam. The propagation of fish is like farmers' hope for their rice and wheat, and they dare not destroy their lives. Therefore, during the two fishing seasons, every fisherman smiles and catches buckets of fish to sell in the town. Those small fish and miscellaneous shrimp are used as wine dishes every night, and everyone lives in peace, as if their lives are only for fishing.

When the peach blossoms are in full bloom, it is again the fishing season for Wengjiazhai. A'gen, a robust man, does not have a wife. There is a mother and a younger sister at home. Today, when he carries his fishing gear out of the house, he tells his eleven-year-old sister: "Don't go out to play randomly. Don't let the wild cats steal the two fish in the wooden bucket!" Singing a song, facing the rising sun, he strides towards the dam. Walking through two mud banks, Jin San comes running towards him, shouting:

"A grave is going to be built on the upper reaches of the Wengjia River. That damned river surface dam has extended by more than ten feet, isn't that going to kill us!" Jin San's face is flushed, and the beads of sweat on his forehead hang down from the corners of his eyebrows on both sides, circling on his red face like two earthworms. Seeing A'gen, it is as if he is a mortal enemy, and he is eager to fight.

"Really building a grave?" A'gen also jumped up. He knew last winter that Jin, the master in town, was going to bury his late grandfather. Yin-yang master Wu Sanguan took his compass every day to examine the left and right sides of the Wengjia Pond. He said that the upper river was a dragon's pool and a tiger's den. If a grave was built there, the descendants would surely prosper. Now they really want to make fengshui on the river surface.

"That murderer! He only knows how to flatter. Why doesn't he recognize Master Jin as his father and come to us for food all the time!"

"Don't talk about that rascal! He has long wanted to dominate the pond!"

"Want us to have no food to eat? He'll have to lose his life first! Let's go to the dam and tell everyone."

Several law-abiding fishermen are already setting up their nets on the dam. Seeing Jin San and A'gen coming, everyone greets them.

"Everyone listen..." Jin San jumps on his own dam like a monkey, "Master Jin is going to build a grave, do you know?..."

Brother Er is the clown of Wengjiazhai. He makes jokes, and when there is something serious, he sneaks away like a ghost. Today, he was the first to arrive at the dam, and he just boasted that he had caught a big fish weighing more than three pounds. Hearing Jin San's speech, he lets out his unique laughter that makes people laugh and shouts to the other side of the river;

"Listen: That dog is inviting our Master Jin to drink a cup of wine!"

Sure enough, laughter like thunder roars from both banks, and some are even applauding.

"Drinking bird wine? We're going to run out of food!" Jin San shouts in an even louder voice: "That murderer is building a grave on the river surface, the river surface dam is ten feet wide, everyone go to the upper river to take a look..." Jin San seems to be going crazy, jumping on the dam, his eyes wide, as if about to burst out of their sockets, staring at Brother Er on the other side of the river.

Everyone knows that Wu Sanguan came to the Wengjia River. Everyone also knows that he called it a dragon's pool and a tiger's den. Brother Er glances at the upper river, where there is a row of wooden stakes straight in the center of the river. He avoids Jin San's line of sight and goes to play with his big fish weighing more than three pounds.

The river is quiet at this time. Only Jin San's voice echoes wildly. Everyone grinds their teeth in hatred. Their hearts are all flying home. They have old mothers, wives, weak younger sisters, and sons. The mouths of the whole family are all facing this pond; now burying the dead on the river is blocking the mouths of the living...

"This... this is an official river..." Several people shout.

"This is an official river! We'll go to the county government to speak out. The magistrate will always be fair!"

"Everyone go together!" Jin San seems to be the leader, ordering.

"We'll all go together!" The voice of the crowd.

Dreams and Reality 209

— Simon

Only dreams can detach us from the coarse and troubled web of life, only dreams can give a comfortable solace to those who dislike the tumultuous affairs of the world. If there is no nourishment of dreams, I think life will appear abnormally dry, or reduce a lot of interest. And it is like a boundless vast desert, full of flying dust and yellow earth obscuring the sky, dreams, it seems, are a very rare oasis in the desert, perhaps a pool of clear water, perhaps a green grass, or perhaps a green house in the distant distance, making the traveler on a long journey find a nest of water to wet his throat in the midst of extreme fatigue, or have a slightly restful place, so as not to become an endless eternal hardship. Although that green house of final rest is still far away, the expectation is naturally brewing, and therefore the heavy steps will unknowingly speed up. Reality is ultimately monotonous and ugly, what is confusing to your eyes is a bleak and terrible picture, on which there are mutual struggles of fighting and shouting, there are the sad groans of being trampled on, there are ferocious faces, there is blood, there are tears, and you yourself are one of the various roles in it. Whoever sees who slips once in a thousand times of attention, they will hit you with a stick, people are aiming so accurately, and you are also aiming so accurately, in daily life everyone hides their true image, and instead pretends to have perhaps a hard or perhaps a weak face to compete and attack the people around them, because life—that is, reality—is a struggle, a tense journey, you can't let go for a moment, and let others step on him. On this treacherous reality—the journey of life, can you take a breath, turn over, and smile?

However, people have to be the agent of life—a prisoner of reality, and the reality of life is simply equal to a cage, a chain, tightly and firmly binding you, restricting you from escaping, all are useless delusions. However, this cage, this chain is invisible, but you know that you can't completely walk out of its circle. If you don't believe it, think about it, how is it that you are always tirelessly running around from morning to night, all year round, grinding, and gradually your hair turns white, your eyes become dim, and you are getting old. Isn't it the result of suffering all kinds of torture in life? So you don't deny at all that the source of the troubles of real life is the abyss of pain, feeling absolute despair, and boredom, like a desert is really too dry. Fortunately, there are dreams, just like there is clear water, green grass, and green houses in the desert, so you will not become an eternally desperate traveler, dreams are beautiful, warm, like a delicate woman with a fragrance all over her body, taking advantage of the period when you temporarily separate from reality—always when your eyes are closed. She smiles and lightly comes to visit you, so you are dizzy and call her to lead you into a splendid, intoxicating paradise, because of her tender comfort and gentle consideration, you can't help but forget all the pain of entanglement in reality, in the dream, you are happy, happy, because you will see the people or things you usually see, and get all kinds of valuable things that you usually can't get, dreams will give you as much as possible without stinginess. And in the dream, you see the real self.

Although it will not heal the sores of reality, but with her comfort, you can get some spiritual relief, temporarily cross the shackles of that painful and troubled web of reality. At the same time, with a degree of injection of dreams, your heart, which is extremely disgusted with reality, will once again support you, like a long-distance traveler expecting the arrival of the distant green house.

Reply to a Listener to Rain 210

— Zhi

Old friend, I haven't seen your writing for a long time, I always thought that you have changed a little, but, I am really gratified, you are still singing your inherent tune. This is what I have always been most impressed with since we met, can you still forget the preface you wrote for me? Over the years, the children who mixed together in childhood have gone their separate ways, the hardships of the world have left absolutely different scars on each of us, but the blood when injured is the same red for everyone, now you can say that the journey has come to an end, and you are resting a little, and I am more and more the opposite of you. I certainly cannot judge whether my current situation is good or bad, but, hearing you sing your inherent unchanging tune from afar, I think privately: should you change your voice?

How can I forget the extravagant travels in Zhenjiang? As for thinking about my unemployment from that time, I don't feel any special sorrow, but, when I occasionally think of a few people who treat friends with a merchant's attitude, I can't help but feel extremely cold. Haven't I seen through the impoverished life of the past two years? It's just a casual mention today.

It is true that I am reading books behind closed doors; it is also true that I am unwilling to be bound by books, in a word, I am indeed "reading books behind closed doors". My reading is neither for the sake of "there are golden houses in books", nor for the old saying "opening a book is beneficial", but for the sake of my wanting to take off the long gown and wear "short clothes" and find a guide. I remember that you wrote an article on "abandoning literature for martial arts" (I certainly can't remember what was said inside), and you expounded on the uselessness of "literature", then you should understand my reading.

We haven't met for a long time, perhaps because I am "reading books behind closed doors"? I have also heard a little about the affairs of your family this time. What else can be said about this? But thinking of my own affairs, I think it is more painful than yours. Let's not talk about it, these old words, let us see what this year's spring is like. Is it necessary to say more? This year's spring is rainy.

You may not believe it, I spent thirty cents last night to see a Chinese-produced sound film, and I was very satisfied to watch it from beginning to end. You will think that I am a low-level enthusiast, and at the same time you will definitely be able to think of the leisurely low-level enthusiast. This, if I said this five years ago, what do you think now? You will definitely be able to answer me that it is "a thought from five years ago."

Let's not mention things from five years ago, or even things from the most current second ago! Come, let us compare what the next five years from today will change to, and answer accordingly.

Opening Piece "Ode to Seeing Off Spring"

An inch of time is worth an inch of gold. An inch of gold cannot buy an inch of time. Time easily passes with spring. As spring leaves, fallen flowers fill the courtyard. Fallen flowers fill the courtyard, flowers do not speak. Courtyard flowers do not speak, locking in the city of sorrow. The city of sorrow surrounds spring without laziness. Without laziness, spring wind carries catkins and dust. Wind and catkins carry dust, lightly unpolluted. Dust lightly unpolluted, grass is green. Green willows hang by the riverbank. Willow thousands of strands dance like catkins. Dancing catkins lightly drift thousands of miles. Drifting thousands of miles to short and long pavilions. Long pavilion to see off spring in the third month. The third month of spring returns, dreams do not form. Dreams do not form, sleep is lazy with spring. Eyes are lazy with spring, accompanied by waning lamps. Waning lamps in a lonely spring boudoir of resentment. Boudoir resentment yellow orioles seem to be telling their feelings. Like telling their feelings, intestines are about to break. Sadness to the point of breaking, a pitiful person. Pitiful people grow old with the spring. Growing old with the spring, fearing to hear the singing of orioles. Fearing to hear the singing of orioles, tear stains wet sleeves at midnight. Midnight listening to two lonely lamps, sipping wine to see off spring under the lamps. Sipping wine to see off spring with a song. A song of spring, emotions of parting. Emotions of parting, the Yangguan willow. Willows dark, flowers bright, another village. When the village birds sing, the southern shore is green. Green waves of spring water rise on the stream banks. Stream banks water rises, reflecting green moss. Moss reflects the remnants of spring, the valley entrance is deep. Deep courtyard butterflies fly, flowers fill the ground. Flying flowers fill the ground, no one sweeps. No one can earn a long spring to stay. Spring stays in Jiangnan, far away to see off. Seeing off writing a song to see off spring.

Shenbao Shanghai Local Supplement Movie Special

The Deep Dark Secrets of Hollywood: Auditioning Actors (Part 2) 214

— Fu

What has been said above pertains to the dark secrets of stage auditions. In Hollywood, there exists a type of actor's agent, essentially a high-class referral service, specializing in connecting actors with various companies. Once a contract is established, they take ten percent of the actor's salary as commission. Of course, for a major star earning three to four thousand dollars a week, the agent pockets three to four hundred dollars in commission weekly, which is quite considerable. But what about the smaller actors? You might think the agent has nothing to gain. But they have their methods. They tell you, secretly: "A certain company is looking for someone through a certain agent, and he doesn't have anyone. I'll recommend you. But... that agent also wants a ten percent commission." You agree, because you're desperate to find a position.

In the end, that "certain agent" situation never existed, but your agent securely pockets twenty percent commission. Sometimes, the so-called "certain agents" number three or more. Your salary is only twenty-five dollars a day, and after paying three or four ten percent commissions, you're only left with enough for transportation. But the enduring hope, that one day you might get a longer engagement, always makes you reluctantly accept, even though you are somewhat aware of the darkness behind it all.

Besides this, there are the dark secrets of the fly-by-night film companies. Once, a small company advertised for student-type actors, to shoot some short films of school life. Someone named Jia went to audition, because he knew he was very knowledgeable about school life and a strong athlete. He arrived there and saw that the so-called company's premises were only temporary, and the director of rehearsals was not difficult to meet. Indeed, he told him that he was exactly the talent they needed. He asked him to send some photos to look at. Of course, he happily agreed.

The next day, he sent the photos. The director looked at them and said, not bad... but... oh, he was too enthusiastic, he absolutely had to help him and make this happen... but it would be best to take a few more photos. Coincidentally, there was a photographer there with deep experience in film, who would certainly know how to take lively and energetic photos. The price wasn't high, only eight dollars a dozen, because that was just the photographer's extra income. Jia thought it wasn't a bad idea, that photos sent to the company must be lively and energetic. Why should he save a little tip and give up a good opportunity? So he made an appointment with the director to take photos the next evening.

When he arrived the next evening, he saw many people dressed as male and female students, like a sophomore dance party. The photographer calculated that there were seventy or eighty people, each paying eight dollars, and the income would be considerable. With a sudden idea, he shrank back, deciding to come back when the senior class had a dance party. Sure enough, one day he met a "female student" he had seen that day. He asked her how it went. It turned out she spent eight dollars and got a dozen small promotional photos. The movie was never made, because the "company closed down."

Radio broadcasting is also a good way to enter the film world, and of course it also has its dark secrets. It is said that a new radio station was about to be established and was recruiting new talent. Jia went again and met a playwriting director. He was extremely polite. He didn't say anything like he was exactly who they were looking for. What he said was, "I can tell genius at a glance. You are one!" He told him that he had already agreed with several large companies, and as long as the program rehearsals were complete, they could sign long-term contracts. But, he had excellent scripts and excellent programs, and there was no problem with the contract, but he had to do three days of auditions first. But... (listen!) In the rehearsals, the director was a person of status, so he had to collect a little subsidy. It wasn't much, only two dollars and fifty cents for each audition. Of course, he wasn't the only one auditioning, but the director told him that others were just trying out, but the contract was exclusively his. He understood in his heart, and immediately excused himself and left.

A few weeks later, he inquired, and the auditions were indeed happening, but whether anyone was listening was a question, because the audition was just like playing a few gramophone records to fill the gaps. He took out a pencil and calculated, thirty people, rehearsing twice a week, charging two dollars and fifty cents each time, (for five weeks, the total would be seven hundred and fifty dollars. Not much, but not bad.

There are really many dark secrets. Varied and numerous, they cannot be generalized. Some use photos to swindle money, others use sound recordings on records to swindle money. When they recruit radio singers, they first ask each person to make a recording for the company to choose. Often someone spends five silver dollars to buy a record worth twenty-five cents. As for finding a job, it's just a wasted trip.

These dark secrets, like Nian Nu in "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio," are full of tricks and impossible to guard against. Fortunately, clever people are always careful. (The End)

Film Commentary

Review of "Flying Generals" 215

— You Jing

“Devil Dogs of the Air”

——Great China Theater

After watching "Flying Generals," one can't help but think of the recently released "Here Comes the Navy." Not only are the main actors in these two films the same, but the script content, presentation style, and production attitude are also completely consistent.

In this era of economic panic and political crisis, suffocating most countries and forcing them to seek unknowable exits in war, the urgency of a second world war has become an undeniable fact. As a result, some playwrights who face reality, feeling the horror of war and caressing the wounds of the first world war, loudly shout out the warning signs of the dangers of war, producing many films that are close to anti-war. Due to differences in the authors' understanding and knowledge, and the profit-driven minds of film enterprises, the works we have seen are either humanistic, passively cursing and exposing the evils of war, or unprincipledly opposing all wars of different natures. Therefore, they only become things that are close to anti-war; but at the same time, there is a group of playwrights who are the mouthpieces of war-makers, the supporters of militarism and militaristic thought, and sing a synchronized quick march to the proposals and actions of expanding armaments and increasing military spending.

From "Here Comes the Navy" to "Flying Generals," is a clear example of this trend. The former boasted of the power of the great navy flying the "Stars and Stripes," and here there is another demonstration of huge aircraft carriers and swarms of planes.

As for the script of the film "Flying Generals," which conveys this mission, it is clearly poor.

Amid the deafening sound of engines and the dazzling shadows of planes, the author presents a rude, wild, frivolous, and arrogant young man named Tom as a hero, making him a sermon for conceit and belligerence. He said that Tom, through the introduction of his neighbor, current military officer Bill Lanigan, entered military training. Because of his improper showboating in flight, he was scolded by his superiors and flew away in his plane. The author forced him to have a problem on the way and land in front of Petty’s coffee shop, giving him the opportunity to brag to the woman, and naturally developed the fictitious plot into romance. Naturally, male and female romances are more interesting as triangles, so first attribute the love of this girl, Quinty, to Bill Lanigan. In this way, using the relationship between superior and subordinate to compete for love, naturally there will be more disputes. He also wrote that Bill Lanigan wanted to inspect Tom's skills, and they rode in the same plane. Then, in the accidental opportunity of the fuselage suddenly catching fire in the air, he wrote that Bill Lanigan jumped with a parachute because he was afraid of death, while Tom landed safely. This artificiality was used to suppress Bill Lanigan and reveal Tom. Then read about them embarrassing each other in Petty's store.

Tom, who suffered a loss in love to his superior, naturally had to work hard in his position, so Tom was finally promoted to adjutant. The main show of the naval exercise and the air force's great mobilization officially opened at this time. Long shots served as a multifaceted performance of the navy and air force, showing off impact, cover, attack, and smoke screens, doing everything possible to demonstrate total power, and then returning to the heroic feats of individual heroes. Tom's wing was broken and he was in danger. At that time, Bill Lanigan was sitting with him again. This time, it was Bill's chance to shine, risking danger to save Tom. It is said that the proud and frivolous Tom was also conquered from then on. So, Bill gave Petty to this young and talented air force hero as a reward, and he was promoted again. Tom and Petty, hero and beauty, were reunited in triumph and good fortune.

Aside from the fictitious story, the far-fetched plot, and the display of the "Stars and Stripes" military power, there seems to be nothing else. If there is anything, it is only the technique of photography.

The director (Lloyd Bacon) also failed to portray the characters' personalities well. Besides writing about Tom's boasting while his companions pretend to sleep, and his manicuring his nails when the officer is instructing him, and his dozing off while planning a battle in a model exercise, the only characteristic is his loud laughter. As for writing about Tom repeatedly wooing Petty and taking pride in being slapped, it was originally the nature of the general foolish sailors. The personality of Petty is even more vague and contradictory. From the time she met Bill Lanigan to his departure, she never showed any love for him, but in the end she suddenly had to make her throw herself into Tom's silly embrace. This process is too lacking.

Most of the actors are from the original cast of "Here Comes the Navy." Their acting skills, other than flying techniques, are extremely limited, so there is no need to say more.

"After Midnight" Is a Sketch of New York Nightlife 216

— Yun Shui

Silver screen heartthrob Clark Gable previously starred with Joan Crawford and Robert Montgomery in "Forsaking All Others." He can deeply perform the active spirit of modern youth to the point of mythologization. But this first collaboration with Constance Bennett in "After Midnight" is also a brand new 1935 romance. Movie fans already know about Constance Bennett's allure. But don't forget that Connie is one of the six movie stars in the world who is most fashionable and elegantly dressed. At the same time, Clark Gable, due to his performance with Claudette Colbert, the star of "It Happened One Night," both won the Academy Award for Best Actor and Actress in 1934.

"After Midnight" was originally Mankiewicz's work. Mankiewicz has served in the press for many years, of course his observations and experiences of New York nightlife are very deep and abundant. Especially regarding the secrets of the East River yacht nightclub Nirety Yacht Club, there are faithful sketches, not to mention the thrilling plots of love disputes between men and women, and assassination detectives, etc.

The director of the film is Robert Z. Leonard. In addition to Clark playing the editor-in-chief of the newspaper and Connie playing the female reporter, other actors include Beery R．Harworth and Stephen, etc.

Welcome Readers to Donate to the Lianhua Expanded Library 217

This newspaper recently received a circular from the translation department of Lianhua Company, saying: "We are writing to inform you that the library group of our company's translation department has been established for more than four years. Recently, due to the concentration of various factories in Xujiahui, the need for book references is even greater than before. Now, the authorities of our company have decided to further expand the original library group and change it to a library. In addition to hiring a special person to manage it, a large number of new books and newspapers will also be ordered for colleagues to read. However, because of the heavy responsibility and limited resources, the collection is still feared to be incomplete. Therefore, we especially send a letter to your newspaper, praying for its publication. Readers who are willing to donate various books, newspapers, magazines, manuals, and other publications are very welcome. Our library will not only keep a special souvenir, but also publish a thank you in Lianhua Pictorial," etc. Readers who wish to donate publications to the Lianhua Library, please send them to the Lianhua Film Company, Triangle Street, Xujiahui, Shanghai.

Movie Novel

Hate Filling the Clouds (Living on Velvet) (2) 218

— Ti Yun

Tolee said, "Your memory is not bad." Ward said again, "As for the money, you had twenty thousand in your bank a year and a half ago. Now I'm afraid you don't even have ten thousand." Tolee interjected, "The exact amount is only about five hundred. Also, there are many unpaid returned checks." Ward listened, feeling dumbfounded, knowing that it was useless to argue or reason with him. He has been like this since the plane crash five years ago.

That was five years ago, he took his parents and sister to Newport in a plane he piloted himself. He encountered a heavy fog midway, and his parents and young sister died, but he escaped death and is still alive today. Although his body is alive, his soul died with those he loved.

That mess was not his fault... because no one could have foreseen that kind of fog. It rose silently and attacked them, like bandits attacking traveling guests. Tolee flew blindly in the fog for several hours. He watched as the gasoline was running out. His parents also knew his mental anguish. Beads of sweat emerged one by one from his forehead. He gritted his teeth and told them that he could only be forced to stop. His parents and sister did not scream, but the terrible expression on their faces was something he could never erase from his mind, because after Tolee finished speaking, the engine had stopped, the plane was spiraling, and plunging into the bottomless abyss.

That was such a happy thing when they set off. The sky was so clear. They all felt excited, knowing that Tolee's driving skills were flawless. But heaven did not fulfill their wishes, and this tragedy happened.

When he woke up in the hospital, he was no longer the Tolee Pike he used to be. Later, he fully recovered. In terms of his body, he had once been a pilot for the air mail bureau, and gradually became famous for not being afraid of death. He had nerves of steel, and the closer he was to death, the happier he became. Day by day, he took risks that sane drivers would not dare to take. These things were well known to Ward Blythe... since that tragedy happened. But he always hoped that his temperament would slowly forget as the years went by. Now, looking at Tolee's spirit, he was deeply worried.

So Ward asked again, "Then what do you plan to do after the five hundred is used up?" He wanted to use money to touch his realistic ideas. But Tolee shrugged and said, "For someone who lives in the clouds, whether or not they have money, how to spend it, is not a problem." Ward advised him, "You're still like this. It's been five years now, you should think it through."

Tolee thought deeply, as if talking to himself, "I know... I have three cracks on my head... but father, mother, and Cynthia..." He paused, feeling a pang of pain in his heart, and then said, "Why should I live? The three people I loved most in the world are dead, but I am lucky enough to live, am I a greedy person who is afraid of death... In fact, my soul died with them long ago... From then on, I will forever live in the clouds." Ward couldn't say a word for a moment, but he was driving the car while thinking deeply. After a while, he reluctantly said, "Of course I understand your feelings, everyone would be like that. But is this kind of meaningless adventure necessary? Why do you have to be like this?" (To be continued)
